Current Commentary

A Word on Developing the Northwest 14

— Shu

Recently, those responsible for politics in our country have mostly been able to focus on the promotion and reform of internal affairs, the advantages and disadvantages of material construction. It has gradually moved from the stage of publicity to the stage of implementation. At this time of serious national crisis and the pressure from powerful neighbors, it can indeed be called a good sign. Recently, such as Song Ziwen, the chairman of the Economic Commission, inspecting the Northwest, and Dai Chuanxian, the president of the Examination Yuan, touring Shaanxi and Gansu, both have far-sighted vision. However, the development of the Northwest has been advocated by the people of the country for several years, and so far there have been no significant achievements. On the contrary, the people of the Northwest have become more and more impoverished. For example, in the Hetao area, after the ravages of war, the fertile land has become barren. In Shaanxi and Gansu, famine is a disaster, and children are regarded as strangers. In Xinjiang, wars are frequent, and hidden dangers are numerous. In Kangzang, political and religious conflicts are not harmonious, and beacon fires rise from time to time. In Sichuan, the Communist Party is causing trouble, and many people are displaced. It can be seen that although the call for developing the Northwest is loud, there are many obstacles ahead, and it is not easy to seek quick results.

Judging from the current situation, the Northwest is a relatively backward region. It has repeatedly suffered from natural and man-made disasters in recent years, and its vitality has almost been destroyed. The people's ability to regenerate themselves is still extremely weak, and it is even more difficult to engage in development. Because the Northwest is located in a remote border area, with a vast territory and sparse population after several periods of turmoil, there are some difficulties in managing agriculture, and it is even more difficult to develop industry. The local military and political authorities only care about their own immediate private interests and do not pay much attention to the hardships of the people's livelihood. Therefore, the rich become poorer and poorer, and the poor have no place to stand. Coupled with obstructed transportation, economic development is very slow, and the people's knowledge is very low. All these factors have a significant impact on the entire Northwest. In short, when it comes to developing the Northwest today, there are several things that deserve the most attention. (1) How to provide the necessary tools for developing the Northwest. This kind of supply should not be limited to money alone. The development is impossible without a large amount of money. At this time of revival from ruins, the concentration of manpower is also an urgent task. The so-called manpower does not only refer to the mentally laborious talents, and general labor talents are also necessary. For example, if the population in the Hetao area is only 50,000, how can they cultivate more than 30,000 square miles of land? The phenomenon of sparse population in Gansu, Xinjiang and other provinces is even more serious. Immigration and garrisoning should not be delayed any longer. The population in the southeastern provinces is excessive, and it seems that they can be moved to the Northwest to make adjustments. However, the climate and living habits in the two places are very different, and the reclamation plan can only be promoted nearby. For example, driving the people of Sichuan and Shaanxi to colonize Gansu and Xinjiang is cheaper in terms of customs, habits and economic organization. (2) In the northwestern provinces, except for Sichuan and Shaanxi, most of them still preserve the economic form of the pastoral era, and handicrafts are not very developed. It will be difficult for them to cope with today's environment. In areas such as Xinjiang and Inner Mongolia, strong neighbors are watching around, and the danger is even greater. Therefore, political measures are more urgent than economic construction. (3) The development of the Northwest cannot but make full use of modern machines. However, before using machines to develop industry, the first thing to know is to study the ability of local handicrafts, and the second is to consider whether it is a productive undertaking that is beneficial to the local people's livelihood. China establishes the nation through agriculture. The Northwest is a vast agricultural and pastoral field. Do not cause the decline and bankruptcy of rural areas due to the deformed development of industry. (4) Reorganizing national defense should not be based solely on military power, but on the entire national economic power. The national defense of the Northwest cannot rely solely on the power of one corner of the Northwest. However, if the development can be successful, it will not only contribute to the national economic power, but also benefit national defense.

The Japanese intelligence agency in Dolon is always trying to get Mongolia. This time, he personally went to Mongolia and felt that to preserve Mongolia, everyone must rise up to study and use the power of the government and society to support it. The 200,000 Mongolian compatriots are serving as the frontier of national defense. This time, he got the impression that there was no time when he was not in danger of being overthrown. (2) Mongolian transportation is centered on Bai Temple, 1,200 miles east to Zhangjiakou, 600 miles east to the Prince De's Mansion near Pangjiang, 600 miles east to Dolon, and about 1,500-1,600 miles west to Ningxia Alxa Banner. The northern border of Outer Mongolia is no more than 600 miles away. The vast grassland can be accessed by cars everywhere. Japan has assembled 100-200 armed vehicles in Dolon, which can ravage the entire Mongolia in a week and complete its dream of a Manchurian-Mongolian empire. (2) The Mongolian system still follows the old system of the Qing Dynasty. This time, Prince De and others felt the danger of being overthrown and began to demand autonomy. However, whether they will have the power to express themselves in the future depends on whether the committee members can unite and become aware. However, it is a question of whether the various banners that have never had political organization can support the critical situation once they are responsible for important tasks. The only task of the Political Council in the future lies in the efforts of the committee members themselves. The league banner political system has not yet taken shape, and the Central Government should generously recognize that it needs assistance and guidance, and should no longer abandon it as before and let it grow and die on its own. Social intellectuals should also form associations to support the Mongolian compatriots. (3) The Mongolian population is at most 200,000. In addition to lamas, women, the elderly and children, there are only 60,000 young men. The reasons for the decline in population are: one is that there are too many lamas, and the other is that the death rate is alarming. Venereal diseases are harmful and should be restricted to religious beliefs and strive for hygiene. (4) Mongolia is still in the nomadic era. Although industry is not developed, it is not without writers. If it is connected with the interior, the economy can also be developed and industry can also be improved. His final hope is that (1) the committee members of the Political Council will unite sincerely and promote Mongolia with all their strength; (2) the government should support Inner Mongolia with economic strength; (3) the society should form groups or specialized research groups to help Mongolia with collective strength. Following the Resignation of the Spanish Cabinet; Political Turmoil Continues to Rise; Parliament Closes Amidst Chaos; Capital City Declares State of Alert 38

Following the resignation of the Lerroux cabinet in Madrid today, political turmoil is developing. This is the seventh political crisis since the collapse of the Spanish Empire. Lerroux's resignation was triggered by President Zamora's attitude of approving the amnesty bill under protest. The President's strongest objection to the bill was the release of 8,000 political prisoners, including thousands of bandits. The police are already struggling to suppress riots today. If the bandits are released, it will further increase the burden on the police. The news of the government's resignation has caused great unrest in political circles. To prevent disturbances, a state of alert has been declared tonight. This is a mild form of martial law. Parliament officially closed after the cabinet crisis occurred. The scene at the time was very chaotic. While the parliamentarians were speaking loudly, the monarchist Maura jumped up and shouted, "Long live the monarchy!" "May it exist forever!" The opposition party unanimously shouted "Long live the Republic!" to drown out Maura's voice. (25th Reuters Telegraph)

With the resignation of the Lerroux cabinet, political turmoil has erupted again. Spanish politicians believe that there are only two ways to resolve the situation: (1) dissolve Parliament; (2) Lerroux would still be responsible for forming a cabinet. President Zamora expressed his opposition to dissolving Parliament, saying that it could lead to civil war, and supported Lerroux's re-forming of a cabinet. (25th Havas Telegraph)

Shifting Clouds in the Far East; US Naval Expansion Cannot Be Delayed; Roosevelt Plans to Request Congressional Appropriations; Vinson Act to be Implemented Soon 42

(Washington) The Vinson Naval Construction Act, which stipulates the construction of 102 warships and 1,184 aircraft, has been passed by both houses of Congress and signed by President Roosevelt on March 27. This law only authorizes the construction of warships in principle. The necessary funding has not yet been discussed. Recently, Roosevelt declared that he plans to request Congress to allocate funds from the public works budget to quickly implement the Vinson Naval Act. The amount of funding requested is undetermined. Roosevelt intends to request $32 million in the fiscal year beginning July 1 of this year to begin construction of 12 destroyers and 6 submarines. The destroyers are intended to replace old ships that have reached the end of their service life. It should be noted that the Vinson Naval Act is completely separate from another naval act passed by Congress last autumn and should not be confused. The naval act passed last autumn allocated a budget of $275 million, also funded by the public works budget, for the construction of two aircraft carriers, one heavy cruiser, three light cruisers, four submarines, and 23 destroyers. Construction of this batch of ships has already begun, and they are all intended to replace old ships. Secretary of the Navy Swanson said that $32 million in funding for the Vinson Naval Act could start construction. Some sources say that Roosevelt's request for Congress to allocate funds to implement the Vinson Naval Act is due to Japan's attitude. If the Vinson Naval Act is implemented, it will be built in stages, with the final batch beginning construction in 1939. Furthermore, a naval conference will be convened next year, which may, as Roosevelt hopes, lead to countries agreeing to limit their navies. This aspect was also taken into consideration when drafting the Vinson Naval Act, so the number of ships built each year was carefully determined to ensure that ships under construction would not be abandoned midway due to a naval conference resulting in limitations on naval construction. (26th Havas Telegraph)

Italian Naval Strength 45

Rome. Italy possesses vast overseas colonies, but does not intend to participate in the prevailing naval competition. Mussolini's intention, although in principle demanding equality with the French navy, it is questionable whether Italy will implement this principle. The Italian-French naval standoff is intended to prevent each other from joining the 1930 British, American, and Japanese naval treaty. Months ago, government authorities declared that they would suspend the 1934 warship building plan. Since then there has been no movement, while France recently decided to start building new warships, including a second-ranked large cruiser with a displacement of 23,000 tons. Italy's naval budget for 1934-1935 is 1,224,780,477 lire, a decrease of 172,441,800 lire from last year, but the value of the US dollar plummeted last year, and the price of the Italian currency is higher than that of the US currency. Currently, each lira is worth about 8.5 US cents, while a year ago it was only worth 5 cents. According to Italian naval authorities speaking to an Associated Press reporter, Italy's naval budget for 1934-35 will be used to maintain the existing fleet and expand naval ports to increase efficiency. Today, Italy's naval policy is only to build new ships to replace old ones, and not to increase the strength and number of the navy. Italy's naval strength includes 2,440 officers and 50,000 soldiers, lower than Britain, the United States, Japan, and France. A list is given below: Two battleships (two others destroyed), two old ironclad cruisers (two others destroyed), six large cruisers, eleven small cruisers (six others under construction), twenty scout ships (large destroyers), thirty-five destroyers, thirty-seven torpedo boats, thirty-one coastal torpedo boats, fifty-five submarines (seven others under construction), one aircraft carrier, seventeen minelayers, thirty-nine minesweepers, nineteen gunboats, forty-three torpedo boat hunters (nine others under construction), and five ironclad gunboats. As for torpedo boat hunters, these are small boats and are not permanently listed. (26th National Telegraph)

American Congressional Silver Faction; Preparing to Duel with Roosevelt; Supporting Compulsory Silver Bill to Raise Silver Prices; Trying Again to Override Presidential Veto 49

(Washington) The silver faction of the House Banking and Currency Committee has now taken action rather than just talking. Today, it took steps to favor the Goldborough Act and the Schullenham Amendment report, forcing the President to find ways to raise silver prices. During a meeting of the Congressional Silver Faction yesterday, it was decided to support the compulsory silver bill rather than the mobile silver bill, hence the vigorous action today. The Goldborough Act advocates the establishment of a Federal Currency Administration to replace the Federal Reserve Bank and manage the issuance of currency. After the committee amended the bill, the Currency Administration would have the power to buy and sell silver, with the goal of keeping the price of 371 and one-quarter cents of silver equal to 23 and 33 hundredths of a cent of pure gold. The Schullenham Amendment stipulates that the Currency Administration is authorized to purchase 50,000,000 ounces of silver per month until 1,000,000,000 ounces have been purchased or the gold-silver ratio reaches 16 to 1. During a meeting between President Roosevelt and congressional silver leaders on April 20, he strongly opposed the wholesale purchase of silver to raise prices through various plans. However, the silver leaders are confident that there is sufficient power in both the House and Senate to pass the bill and amendment. They are also well aware that a two-thirds majority is required to override the President's veto. However, since Congress has already overridden the President's veto of the independent agency funding bill, the silver leaders believe that once they have done it once, they might as well try again and fight a worthwhile battle for silver. The House has already passed the Dies Act by a large majority and sent it to the Senate Committee. The silver faction in the Senate now plans to propose an amendment to nationalize silver. (25th National Telegraph)

Dai Chuanxian Returns to Nanjing; Recounts Impressions of Western Trip 52

(Nanjing) Dai Chuanxian, President of the Examination Yuan, completed his inspection of the Northwest and returned to Nanjing on the afternoon of the 26th. Those who came with him included Wang Yingyu, Xu Chonghao, and secretaries and doctors. Jiao Yitang and Barger of the Air Survey Team of the General Staff Department did not return because they had to meet Song Ziwen in Xi'an. After Dai got off the train, he crossed the river into the city and returned to the Examination Yuan's official residence to rest and organize the inspection documents, preparing to draft an inspection report and submit it to the National Government within a few days, along with his opinions, as a reference for planning the development of the Northwest. He also has inspection notes that will be sent to various newspapers for publication to draw the attention of the Chinese people to the Northwest. At 5:00 PM, National Government Chairman Lin personally visited and did not leave until after an hour. Lin inquired in detail about the current situation in the Northwest and the matter of Xi'an as a secondary capital. Dai plans to rest for a day or two and then go to Hangzhou to participate in the Kalachakra Dharma Assembly. Reporters visited Dai and were received by Wu Xinheng, who accompanied him back to Nanjing, who described his impressions of this trip, saying that the impression of this trip to the Northwest was better because the bandit disasters of the past have gradually returned to their former state. The Northwest Agricultural and Forestry College has held its founding ceremony, and the school buildings are under construction, but due to the large scale of the project, it will not be possible to start school until next year. On the 24th, he met Song Ziwen in Luoyang and only talked at the station for five hours. Dai provided Song with his inspection experience for reference. Due to time constraints, Song will only stop in Xi'an, and plans to postpone his trips to Qinghai and Ningxia. The result of this inspection is that the primary development of the Northwest should first focus on water conservancy. In addition, transportation and highways are also necessary. (26th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Dai Chuanxian, together with Xu Chonghao, Wang Yingyu, and others, arrived in Nanjing by special train on the afternoon of the 26th. Staff from the Examination Committee, Selection Committee, and Evaluation Department of the Examination Yuan crossed the river to welcome them. After Dai got off the train and crossed the river, he entered the city and returned to his private residence to rest. Chairman Lin visited Dai at 4:00 PM to discuss his impressions of the trip to the West. According to Dai, those who visited him, due to the limited time, he was unable to stay longer in Gansu and Qinghai to broaden his horizons, which he greatly regretted. However, through this trip, he became acquainted with people from various places, which will make it easier to travel again in the future. As for his feelings, in general, it can be said that this was the first satisfying trip since leaving home at the age of fifteen. The various ethnic groups in the Northwest live together, and those who discuss this often consider the ethnic issue to be very difficult to resolve. This can be said to be a major misconception of those who do not read modern books and do not digest them. The various ethnic groups in the Northwest are no more than different surnames in the interior. Just as different surnames can coexist and progress together, why can't different ethnic groups integrate? What is especially felt is that this time Xian believes that he is just returning to his hometown to visit old friends, and not traveling far away. Everyone says that trees have roots and water has sources. The great waters of China are none other than the Yellow River and the Yangtze River, which both originate in Qinghai. This shows that the various ethnic groups in the Northwest and the Han people are originally one family. They have long lived in their hometown, while we have developed abroad. As for religion, language, and writing, they are only things that have evolved over thousands of years of history and have nothing to do with whether races are the same or different. As for the Mongol, Tibetan, Hui, and Han nationalities seen in Xining, all have a spirit of progress, which is truly gratifying. In particular, the art and architecture of Gansu and Qinghai are especially admirable, and the beauty and intelligence of the people of Lanzhou are no less than those of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. In the future, as long as transportation and water conservancy are handled properly, they will naturally move forward step by step. The great unified civilization and new life of China are in the Northwest, which is why this trip has strengthened my belief. As for the Agricultural and Forestry College, the foundation has now been laid. As long as those in charge do the work practically, it is determined that it can be successful. As for its relationship with the local area, let alone the future, even now, the disaster victims in Wu and Mei counties have already benefited significantly. Anyone in Shaanxi must be able to say this, without the need for further discussion. Because I am a little tired from the long journey, I plan to rest for two days before going to Hangzhou to participate in the Dharma Assembly. (26th Central News Agency)

The Judicial Yuan: Examples of Divorce Conditions 54

The term "abuse that makes cohabitation unbearable" is not limited to physical harm; mental anguish that renders cohabitation intolerable also constitutes abuse. While a spouse subjected to such abuse may seek divorce, the abuse must reach the level of making cohabitation unbearable. Minor altercations or instances of assault that are followed by reconciliation and forgiveness do not constitute grounds for divorce, and cannot be used as the basis for a divorce petition. Guidelines for People's Organizations 65

(Nanjing) At its 118th meeting on the 26th, the Central Standing Committee passed the following guidelines for people's organizations: 1) Farmers' associations, fishermen's associations, chambers of commerce, industry and commerce guilds, women's associations, cultural organizations, educational associations, and charitable organizations shall be guided and conducted in accordance with their respective existing laws and regulations. 2) Ordinary labor unions shall be guided and conducted in accordance with the existing Labor Union Law. If there are special circumstances in labor unions below the county and city levels, local party and government organs may, for the sake of unified guidance and supervision, establish a general organization with the approval of the central government. 3) Special labor unions, with the exception of the Chinese Seamen's Union, which should be guided and conducted in accordance with existing laws and regulations, the party headquarters should, as appropriate, participate in the guidance of railway, postal, and telecommunications unions before their respective laws and regulations are implemented. 4) Student organizations within schools shall be guided and conducted in accordance with the Organizational Outline of Student Self-Government Associations for the time being. Other organizations outside of schools should be seriously investigated by the local higher party headquarters. If it is deemed necessary to establish them, they may be permitted to register for record after special permission is obtained, and personnel should be dispatched to provide guidance at any time. 5) Religious organizations, public welfare organizations, free professional organizations, and other special social groups, with the exception of religious organizations which may be governed by cultural organization laws and regulations, shall be governed by existing laws and regulations if they have separate laws and regulations. The rest shall be handled in accordance with the revised organizational plan for people's organizations, after careful consideration. (Central News Agency, 26th)

Inside Story of German Rumors About Recognizing Manchukuo: Spring Sunshine Hall Berlin Correspondence: Rumors Released by the Japanese Side; German Authorities Issue Denials 91

For more than a month, rumors about Germany's imminent recognition of the puppet organization have been rampant. European newspapers have published many conflicting reports on this matter. After the embassy in Germany made many inquiries and questioned the German government, it learned the content of the matter. Here is a special description:

The most noteworthy information obtained from Berlin includes the following two: (1) A Japanese Joint News Agency report stated that negotiations on German-Manchurian economic issues have begun in Tokyo. German Ambassador to Japan Dircksen, German Embassy staff member Kroll, who recently returned to Japan after inspecting Manchuria, and German Consul to Harbin Balser all participated. It was also said that Kroll's staff will return to Berlin on March 1 and report on the issue of Germany's recognition of Manchukuo at this time. (According to this news, it was seen in the Berlin Daily on February 17, 1934, which was based on news from Amsterdam. The news released by the Japanese Club in Germany on February 17 was also the same. It can be seen that this news was indeed released by the Japanese side.) (2) The Berlin Germania newspaper reprinted a report from the London Financial Times on February 21 of this year. The newspaper's correspondent in Tokyo stated that the plan of Germans to obtain an economic base in Manchuria has failed. Japanese and French industrial investment groups in Manchuria will sign an agreement, but Germany has not been able to participate. Eighteen months ago, General Von Seeckt had planned to supply Manchuria with military supplies, but was rejected by Manchukuo. On September 10 last year, Colonel Ott, the German military attaché to Japan, went to Manchuria with a personal letter from German Chancellor Hitler to discuss the issue of recognizing Manchukuo and requesting certain patents from Manchuria to Germany. Because this plan failed, German businessmen have left Manchuria one after another, and only the Stinnes Company is still there.

According to the above two pieces of news, not only the Chinese side is deeply uneasy, but even the Germans who usually sympathize with the Chinese side are also quite worried. The embassy in Germany has repeatedly questioned the German Foreign Ministry and inquired from other parties. As a result, it was learned that this news was all groundless.

(1) Regarding the news about German-Manchurian relations published in the Berlin Daily mentioned above, the embassy in Germany ordered Counselor Tan Boyu to informally visit the responsible personnel of the German Foreign Ministry. According to the reply, it was all false. However, German Consul to Harbin Balser did stay in Tokyo, but there was no mission. Also, Balser went to Japan via Honolulu to meet his son on a German warship. As for the matter of Kroll's staff returning to Berlin to report, it was even more unfounded. (According to this news, it was seen in Information No. 337 released by the Japanese Club in Germany on February 17 of this year.)

(2) On February 26 of this year, the German News Agency, Deutsche Machrichtns Buro, released a message saying that rumors have been spreading recently that Germany will recognize Manchukuo. After checking the rumors, responsible parties stated that they were rumors created by people with ulterior motives and completely inconsistent with the facts. On the same day, the Berlin Broadcasting Station also spread the same news. Major German newspapers also published the same news. The Berlin Germania newspaper reprinted an article from the German Diplomatic Political News Agency on February 22, refuting the article about [Germany and Manchuria], which was even more blatant. The article stated that it was true that a staff member of the German Embassy in Japan had once gone to Manchuria to investigate business matters. As for General von Seeckt, although he had been to Manchuria, it was only in a private capacity. As for Colonel Ott, there was no such thing as going to Manchuria with a personal letter from the German Chancellor. German commercial firms in Manchuria are all operating normally and are not related to the Japanese and French investment groups.

Based on a comprehensive observation of the above news, the move of Germany to recognize the puppet organization will not be realized for a while. Moreover, a responsible German person once said that the Japanese have made sacrifices of blood and flesh for Manchuria and will never seek benefits for others. After careful analysis of this statement,

Even if Germany is unwilling to stay out of the Manchurian market due to economic relations, but weighing the pros and cons, Germany will definitely not be the first to recognize the puppet organization, it can be asserted.

Japan is Building Seven Major Railways in Northeast China (Harbin Correspondence): Obviously to Deal with the Soviet Union; Completely Handled by the South Manchuria Railway; All with Military Implications; Deployment in the Greater Khingan Mountains; Stationing Troops in the Wuling Mountains 92

The Japanese army stationed along the Chinese Eastern Railway has packed up their luggage and is preparing to return. They are called triumphant, and everyone has smiles on their faces. We have endless unspoken suffering, and even more powerful troops - the Nagoya Division - have been replaced. What is their intention? People here have generally understood that it is to deal with the Soviet Union. However, the Japanese army knows that it is not enough to rely solely on military force to fight. What's more, modern warfare requires a huge army and a powerful transportation system to support it. The three northeastern provinces do indeed have criss-crossing railways, which are almost sufficient, but they are not enough to confront the Soviet Union. Therefore, it has now been decided to immediately build seven railways. The routes are as follows:

(1) Mudanjiang to Jiamusi Railway

(2) Lingyuan to Chengde Railway

(3) Yebaishou to Yifeng Railway

(4) Erzhan to Heihe Railway

(5) Changchun to Dalai Railway

(6) Dalai to Taonan Railway

(7) Huaiyuan to Solon Railway

These seven routes have been agreed upon by the Japanese and the Kwantung Army in the puppet government of Changchun. The South Manchuria Railway Company is responsible for the construction. (We must know that the South Manchuria Company is equivalent to the British East India Company, and it is not an ordinary enterprise or commercial organization.)

The estimated project cost is 140 million Japanese yen. Needless to say, the construction materials are entirely supplied by Japan or companies affiliated with the South Manchuria Railway.

On the surface, this seems to be an economic undertaking, but it is not. First, look at the Lingyuan to Chengde Railway. Not only will it control the entire province of Rehe, but it also has a conspiracy to peep into Chahar in the west and harass Hebei in the south based on the shape of the Wuling Mountains. As for the line from Yebaishou to Chifeng, outsiders mostly believe that its intention is to seize local gold mines and other products. In fact, this is still a secondary meaning. The most important thing is to advance into Inner Mongolia, while also having the intention of invading Outer Mongolia as an attachment.

Secondly, there is the railway along the Mudanjiang River from Mudanjiang Station via Yilan to Jiamusi. In the past, Japan's operation of the Northeast focused all its efforts on South Manchuria. In North Manchuria, it has not been able to control the Chinese Eastern Railway. Now, the Jihui Railway is almost a success, and the line from Tumen to Mudanjiang is also about to be completed. However, the Japanese have no guarantee for the immigration of the Songhua River coast, and there is no preparation for military transportation in northeastern Jilin. Therefore, this railway must be built quickly. On the one hand, it can establish an economic foundation for invading North Manchuria, and on the other hand, it also increases the convenience of attacking the Soviet Union's Primorsky Krai.

Again, is Japan's military plan for the Soviet Union. Although it has not been completely determined, in the offensive defense of North Manchuria, the border fortress of Manzhouli is not something that can be borrowed in modern military affairs. Deploying defenses along the Heilongjiang River is both easy to suffer losses and will cause current difficulties. Therefore, after several inspections by the Kwantung Army, it was finally decided to take the Greater Khingan Mountains as the first line of defense against the Soviet Union in the west. Solid fortresses are currently being built. Changchun to Dachar, Dalai to Taonan, and Huaiyuan to Solon are mainly intended to facilitate the construction of defense fortifications in the Greater Khingan Mountains. In the event of an incident in the future, there will be another tool that can be used, and the Xilin Gol League can also be seized from the side to enter the eastern part of Chahar. This is a two-sided conspiracy of Japan.

Also, the road from Erzhan to Heihe directly shoots at Hailanpao on the opposite bank of the Heilongjiang River. If you want to use this road to break the connection between the Ussuri Railway and Siberia with heavy troops, it will be easier for him to attack Vladivostok. At the same time, if he can achieve his desired goals in order, Tokyo and Osaka can reduce the threat of air strikes. Therefore, he is very

Focus on the construction of this railway, to create its offensive strength in a short period of time, to let his iron hand touch the Soviet Union. As for the decision of victory or defeat, I am afraid that it is still in the hands of the person standing on the side, and it is not known. (April 17)

Jilin Puppet Authorities Forcibly Buy People's Land: City Residents Severely Oppressed and Forced to Obey; Villagers Refuse to Yield and Join the Righteous Army 93

Jilin Correspondence: Japanese troops abuse the people of Northeast China in every possible way. All their cunning schemes are carried out by the puppet authorities under Japanese orders, ostensibly to avoid their notorious reputation. However, their ferocious wolf-like faces are ultimately exposed. For example, this time they forcibly purchased land in Jilin. In the cities, residents had no choice but to obey and had no way to resist. However, the farmers in the countryside all had firearms and sought survival in death, rising up in resistance. Thereupon, the Japanese disregarded everything and used airplanes and artillery to massacre the villagers, leveling seventeen villages, a tragedy too horrible to bear. The following details are recorded:

The puppet Jilin Municipal Preparatory Office, under Japanese orders and in the name of consolidating port affairs, arbitrarily forcibly bought civilian land in the commercial port area, numbered it, and released it for construction, revising the regulations for renting and building in the commercial port. The method for purchasing civilian land was decided by the puppet port affairs committee, with the majority of the civilian-owned vacant land east of the commercial port's main road being considered suitable for acquisition, as it was located in important locations. West of the main road, only a small portion of land belonging to the Li family in Qingnianhui East Hutong, as well as the Fan and Guan families outside Beixin Kai Gate, the Xiao family outside Bahu Gate, and several parcels of vacant land such as the Huiyuan Distillery west of Chalu Kou, were to be included in the acquisition. All other areas were not to be acquired at this time. A list of the areas to be acquired this time was posted, and all landowners on the list were not allowed to prepare for construction or cultivation. All land deeds and title deeds for the listed lands were to be submitted to the office by April 30th to obtain receipts, so that personnel could be dispatched to measure the area together with the landowners and then set a date to issue prices according to regulations. As for the scattered small parcels of civilian land and houses outside the list but along suitable routes, which must be acquired for the sake of consolidating port affairs, it was planned to notify the landowners to acquire them according to regulations after they were determined.

The Japanese and puppet Jilin provincial authorities, having adopted the method of acquiring land from the citizens of Jilin, again applied it to the Yilan area in northeastern Jilin, the former defense zone where General Li Du led his troops in a desperate battle against the Japanese army. They declared the area as a reclamation zone, and all original landowners had to accept the acquisition according to the method of acquiring civilian land. The people of the area, nurtured by the spirit of resisting Japan, were extremely resistant. They also discovered that the authorities only issued receipts for the land deeds and title deeds they first collected, which was the same step as acquiring civilian firearms. Thereupon, public sentiment was in an uproar, and hundreds of villages spontaneously united, gathering over a thousand strong young men with guns. Resolving to fight to the death rather than surrender, they first killed or dispersed their wives and children, then launched a swift attack on the nearby Japanese troops, killing over two hundred and fifty Japanese. For a time, the Japanese and puppet authorities in the provincial capital were very frightened and dispatched over thirty airplanes, as well as artillery, to bomb the area. It is estimated that the seventeen villages that first initiated the uprising were completely reduced to rubble, a scene too tragic to witness. Afterwards, the Japanese realized that the method they had adopted was inappropriate, as it had aroused a popular uprising. They urgently kept it secret, prohibiting any publicity, and few outsiders knew about it. Currently, the thousand-plus people have formed a volunteer army. As it is difficult to resist the enemy, they have retreated to the mountains and are temporarily stationed there.

Jiangxi Headquarters: Strictly Prevent Abuse of the Blockade, Measures for Dealing with Illegal Goods 100

Nanchang Correspondence: The Jiangxi Headquarters, in accordance with the methods for blockading bandit areas, stipulates that all transportation of military supplies must be submitted to the highest military authority to which they belong for approval and issuance of permits or certificates before they can be inspected and released. Those without permits will be detained by local military police teams. Transportation of daily necessities requires a certificate or permit that can provide responsible proof before it can be allowed to pass; otherwise, it is absolutely prohibited. The above methods did not clearly stipulate how to handle goods seized without permits or certificates, or goods that did not match the certificates. Such cases have always been handled by weighing the circumstances, carefully considering the facts of the crime within the scope of the law, and providing appropriate treatment. While striving for strict blockade, considerable consideration was given to the convenience of the people, originally hoping for minimal disturbance to the people and effective results. Recently, because the defined words [detention] [prohibition] were too vague, the handling in various places differed, resulting in numerous abuses. Some confiscated without authorization, some released on bail, some confiscated goods and then fined, and some confiscated goods and imprisoned the person. Various malpractices were endless. If not clearly stipulated, how can fairness be shown and the blockade emphasized? Therefore, two points of measures are specially stipulated for subordinates to comply with: (1) Military supplies and supplies aiding bandits seized in violation of the methods for blockading bandit areas shall be confiscated and dealt with according to law, and the perpetrators shall be punished in accordance with Special Law and Common Criminal Law according to the identity of the offender and the circumstances of the crime, in accordance with Instruction No. 1417 of this headquarters. (2) For daily necessities without permits or certificates or with non-compliant permits, or with goods that do not match the permits, if there is no suspicion of aiding the bandit area, 20% of the transported goods will be confiscated for public use. The distribution standard is half to the personnel who made the breakthrough and half to local public welfare undertakings. The remaining items will be ordered to be sold locally, without any release, to show punishment and emphasize the blockade, and the purchaser's certificate must be obtained and submitted for assessment to prevent abuse. (April 23)

Jiangnan: Seawall Construction to Begin Soon, Construction Department Formulates Tendering Implementation Measures 103

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The situation of the Jiangnan seawall is precarious. The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department has surveyed and proposed a main project plan to select urgent parts to start construction according to the amount of funds available. The various situations have been略誌 (briefly recorded) in the previous report. It is now heard that the Jiangnan Dike Engineering Office of the department has prepared all the procedures for the previous project. The required wood piles and stone materials have been advertised for business to bid and contract. Businesses with the required material handling experience and capabilities can go to the department to領取标单 (collect bidding forms) and other documents from now until the 29th of this month, and bid according to regulations. The bidding will be opened in public at 10 am on the 30th of this month in the department's auditorium. In order to慎重 (ensure careful consideration) the project, the department has detailed招標章程 (tendering regulations), 办料细则 (material handling details), 施工细则 (construction details) and other types of rules. All 投標 (bidding)去取标凖 (selection standards), 工料 (work and materials) 騐收方法 (inspection methods), and 工程实施方法 (project implementation methods) are clearly defined. The important points are extracted as follows: (1) The value of the seawall's 工料 (work and materials) will be strictly investigated on-site in the market by personnel dispatched by the Construction Department. After the bidding is opened, the bidders who offer reasonable prices, have rich experience, and sufficient capital will be selected and announced as the winning bidder and the alternate winning bidder. (2) The招商承攬 (business contract) will be prepared in triplicate as usual, plus an additional copy to be posted in the Seawall Engineering Office. (3) When the wood is transported to the 工時 (construction site), the 騐收員 (inspector) will inspect, circle, and register the number逐一 (one by one) according to the specified quality, length, and circumference, and the contractor will arrange and積 (stack) them in the designated location. (4) When the stone is transported to the 工時 (construction site), the 監工員 (supervisor) will逐船騐收 (inspect each ship), and the contractor will transport and unload them at the designated time and mark a landmark for identification. The stone transport ships must be numbered one by one, and their 标凖容石量 (standard stone capacity) and 标凖载运吃水深度 (standard loading draft depth) must be measured. The draft line must be clearly marked with red paint or other equivalent methods, and listed separately for verification. (5) Each time the stone is inspected, the 監工員 (supervisor) may randomly designate a location to order the stone transporters to翻去 (turn over) the stones on top to inspect whether there are架空 (voids) and mixed 풍화 (weathered) inferior stones. If there are the above 情弊 (malpractices), they will not be inspected, and they will be instructed to correct the errors and replace them before re-inspection. (6) If any 工員役 (workers) demand 私費 (private fees) from the contractor, the contractor may report by name at any time. If any bribing is found, both parties will be strictly dealt with according to law.

Suzhou: Rickshaw Pullers' General Strike, Disorder Occurs on Guanqian Street 105

All 3,500 rickshaw pullers in Suzhou, due to the recent decision of the Public Security Bureau's Bureau Affairs Conference to ban rickshaws, stipulating that empty cars are not allowed to be dragged arbitrarily on the streets, believing that they cannot solicit passengers and that it hinders their livelihoods, suddenly launched a general strike yesterday (26th) morning at 6:00 AM. They first released the air from all the car tires, and then, in groups of hundreds,阻 (obstructed) 自备 (self-owned)包车 (chartered cars) passing through the main areas 　二三分所 (the second and third branch stations of)巡官 (patrol officer) Wang Xunxiang led the police to persuade them without success, so they telephoned the Public Security Bureau. Bureau Chief Shen Gao　immediately dispatched a row of Flying Patrol Team, led by 巡官 (patrol officer) Xie Huaiqing to Guanqian, and arrested the leading rickshaw pullers. At that time, it was already past 9:00 AM, and Guanqian gathered six or seven hundred rickshaw pullers. Seeing the Flying Patrol Team arresting people, they 包围 (surrounded) and 殴打 (beat) the guards. 巡官 (patrol officer) Wang, et al. were also beaten. 巡官 (patrol officer) Liu was cuffed on the neck with a 麻绳 (hemp rope) and dragged along the road. Liu, being outnumbered, opened fire with a 朝天手枪 (pistol pointed upwards). The Flying Patrol Team also fired 盒子炮 (box cannons). For a time, the order was 혼란 (chaotic). Guanqian Street shops immediately closed their doors. It opened in half an hour. As a result, rickshaw pullers Qi Xiaoyou (25 years old) and Liang　Cai (25 years old) were shot. Qi was more seriously injured in the knee, and Liang was injured in the head. They were sent to Guangmin Hospital to extract the bullets. At that time, each branch station received the news, and the officials and police immediately dispatched all of them and strictly enforced martial law, but the street police in　门 (　門) Ma Road, Guanqian, and Jingde Road were beaten. The police have arrested 12 rickshaw pullers, including Zhu Huailong and Xue Yinshan, and taken them to the bureau. The crowd then dispersed. Also, when the rickshaw pullers were on strike and occurred disorder, lawyer Li Mian took a 自备 (self-owned)包车 (chartered car) to the court and was beaten by the strikers when he passed Guanqian Street. The侦缉队 (detective team) also detained He Jue, who was suspected of instigating the labor tide. The officials believed that the cause of the labor tide was the sudden onset and that there was or was not an organization in advance. The reason may not only be to ban拖空车 (dragging empty cars). Therefore, the investigation is currently being carried out with all efforts to determine the background and to find the main actors. After the disorder in Guanqian Street, the Public Security Bureau, the County Party Headquarters, the Rickshaw Rental Industry Association, and various rickshaw companies dispatched personnel to mediate and handle the situation. The county magistrate and the County Party Headquarters gathered the rickshaw pullers at the Party Headquarters at 5:00 PM. As a result, the rickshaw pullers had agreed to resume work today (27th). Last night, the military and police were heavily guarded. The Second Division of the Army stationed in Suzhou was stationed in the city and there was no accident.

Silk Factory Wage Demands 107

In recent years, silk factories have been in a slump, many have closed, and wage demands from workers have been frequent. The Taisheng Silk Factory outside the East Gate was leased last year by Zhang Mingzhai from Shanghai and started operations, with Chen Jinsan, the owner of Chen Yixing Game Store at Tonghui Bridge, guaranteeing the rent and wages. Unexpectedly, it closed down not long after starting, owing the female workers ten days' wages. The female workers repeatedly demanded payment without success, so yesterday afternoon, more than fifty of them gathered and surged to Chen Yixing Game Store to find the guarantor, Chen Jinsan. However, the front of the game store was Hongtaixing Sauce and Fermented Grains Shop, owned by Gao Yangchen. Seeing the female workers rush in, Gao immediately closed the shop door and telegraphed the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau to send police to suppress the situation, bringing all the female workers and Gao Yangchen to the bureau. A strong officer interrogated them, and the female workers accused Gao Yangchen of letting Chen Jinsan escape, but Gao vehemently denied it. As a result, the officer ordered Gao to hand over Chen Jinsan within five days, and the matter came to a temporary end.

Temple Fair in Baitaxiang Causes Great Disaster in Changzhou 108

The Baitamiao Temple in Baitaxiang, the third district of Wuyi County, recently planned to hold a theatrical performance and a temple fair. The district head, Chen Yi, telegraphed the county government to send police to stop it. County Magistrate Cai dispatched Zhuang Zhenying, the first squad leader of the first squadron of police, and Gu Xiangnong, the second squad leader, leading thirty officers, to the village on the 23rd to prohibit the theatrical performance. Squad Leader Zhuang and others planned to return to Changzhou on the 24th, but were then ordered to prohibit the Baitaxiang temple fair on the 25th. That morning, Squad Leader Zhuang was at Zheng Lu Bridge, where District Head Chen Yi met with the police and patrol officers from the Public Security Sub-bureau. They were about to proceed to stop the fair when the Baitamiao temple fair also arrived at the town of Sanhekou. District Head Chen then questioned the village head, asking why, after guaranteeing to stop the fair, it was being held again. At that moment, the ignorant people at the fair attempted to make trouble for the district head. Squad Leader Zhuang stepped forward to dissuade them and prevent violence, but the broadsword team in the gathering carried firearms. Seeing Squad Leader Zhuang raise his hand, they suspected he was about to fire a gun, and the broadsword team fired first, piercing Squad Leader Zhuang's sleeve. At this point, the police also fired into the air, and the order was instantly disrupted. District Head Chen Yi was beaten by the villagers in the chaos and then taken away. The whereabouts of the clerk of the Public Security Sub-bureau are still unknown. The police tried their best to suppress the situation, and the villagers dispersed. Squad Leader Zhuang and others urgently tried to rescue District Head Chen, but after many inquiries, there was no clue. They then telegraphed the county government. County Magistrate Cai sent another team to the village to join the rescue effort. It was then learned that District Head Chen had been beaten severely, covered in blood, and his life was in danger. He was still tied up by the villagers inside the Baitamiao Temple. Whether the police have rescued him is still unknown.

Autopsy of Feng Peisan in Zhenjiang 109

After Yangzhong County Magistrate Feng Peisan was re-coffined the night before, his nephew, Feng Jiafan, received the bad news in Yangzhong and rushed there overnight. By the time he arrived, the coffin had already been sealed. Feng, believing that the cause of death, whether murder or suicide, was suspicious, advocated for an autopsy to dispel doubts and clarify the truth. He reported to the authorities and requested an examination. At 7:00 PM yesterday (the 25th), the court sent an examining magistrate to where Feng's coffin was placed. Workers pried open the coffin lid, removed the cement, and lifted Feng's body out, placing it on the coffin lid. Feng's face color was slightly changed, and blood still flowed from his nostrils. The examining clerk Shen then untied the clothes on the corpse and carefully inspected the entire body. Feng's family members observed the examination next to the body. It was determined that Feng's corpse only had a slight injury to the right hip bone, which had been pierced by something. The bloodstains on the back of the head and jaw were all accumulated blood flowing from the nose, not wounds. The abdomen was slightly elevated, containing water. Observing this shape, it was determined that he had drowned before death. After the examination, Feng signed and fingerprinted the corpse collection form and re-coffined the body.

Robbers of a Navigation Boat Executed by Firing Squad in Jiangyin 110

On the 7th of this month, a night navigation boat from Huashu, the ninth district, to Wuxi, passed through Dujia Bridge when the boat owner discovered that there were four robbers hiding on board. He reported to the local security corps, who searched the boat. The robbers opened fire and resisted arrest, killing villager Hou Sanbao on the spot and wounding passengers Wang Hongbao and group member Wang Kunyuan. Group members Hua Zicai and others apprehended the robbers Zhao Kesheng and others and handed them over to the county for questioning. They confessed without hesitation and were reported to the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs according to the Bandit Suppression Law. After approval by telegram from the provincial government, County Magistrate Bao ordered the police to bring the two robbers, Zhao Kesheng and Jiang Yude, to the Lujiafen execution ground outside the North Gate and execute them by firing squad at 11:00 AM on the 25th.

City Government Order: Relief for Shanghai's Cotton Industry; Orders Finance and Social Bureaus to Devise Methods; Authorities Solicit Opinions from Cotton Industry Peers 113

According to the Guomin News Agency, Shanghai's cotton industry has always been known for its development, but recently, due to the dumping of foreign cotton, the domestic cotton market has plummeted. Furthermore, current inventories are piling up, and sales are stagnating. Although the Cotton Industry Association has discussed relief measures, due to the prevailing environment, no solution has been found. The Cotton Industry Association previously submitted a petition to the Ministry of Industry of the Executive Yuan, requesting prompt relief. The Ministry of Industry repeatedly sent personnel to Shanghai to investigate and consult with the local Cotton Industry Association on relief measures. It is learned that the Executive Yuan has ordered the Shanghai Municipal Government to find ways to provide relief. Yesterday, the city government ordered the Social and Finance Bureaus to promptly devise relief measures. It is said that the authorities believe that Shanghai is an industrial center and that relief for the cotton industry is urgent. Currently, in addition to resisting the dumping of foreign cotton, cooperation among industry peers is necessary. It is said that the local cotton industry peers will be convened within days to solicit relief measures.

Thirty Million Yuan in Securities to Be Issued by the Government; Ministry of Finance Sends Personnel to Shanghai for Consultation 114

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the Yigeng Indemnity Loan Syndicate, organized by sixteen banks including the Central Bank in Shanghai, included in its 44 million yuan loan contract with the Ministry of Finance that the syndicate would be allowed to issue 30 million yuan in securities to recover a portion of the loan. Recently, the Ministry of Finance observed that the money market in Shanghai was loose, and the banks did not need to urgently recover cash. It has sent personnel to Shanghai to consult with the banks on amending the contract to have the Ministry of Finance directly issue the securities. A Shenshi News Agency reporter investigated the details as follows:

Consultation by Ministry of Finance 115

The Ministry of Finance, during the Fujian Incident, needed a large amount of funds and had no choice but to use the Yigeng Indemnity refund funds to borrow 44 million yuan from sixteen banks, including the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, in Shanghai. Both parties entered into a contract on January 27 of this year, and Article 11 stipulated that the syndicate could [issue securities worth 30 million yuan at once]. At the time, the syndicate believed that the amount of the loan was very large, and the banks were deeply concerned about the impact on finance. To avoid illiquidity and financial stagnation, they made this request to reserve room for adjustment. Now, the Ministry of Finance believes that during this season of tea and silk sales, the money market in previous years was already very tight, but now, with the decline in international trade, the need for cash is not high, and the banks are still very loose. There is no need to issue this public debt. Therefore, it has specially dispatched Section Chief Xu of the Public Debt Department to Shanghai to consult with Zeng Rongpu, the secretary-general of the syndicate, and the relevant banks to change the issuance of public bonds to be done directly by the Ministry of Finance to save on procedures.

Syndicate Meeting 116

The sixteen banks, including the Central Bank, consulted with the personnel sent by the Ministry of Finance and believed that it was possible to reach an agreement. Yesterday, they convened a meeting of representatives from each bank at the Bank Club. Sixteen people attended, including Li Fusun, Xi Demao, Tang Shoumin, Song Ziliang, Hu Bijang, and Bei Songsun. After discussion, the decision was unanimously passed. However, the banks incurred considerable losses in preparing for the issuance, and no one was willing to take responsibility for compensating them. After consultation, the Ministry of Finance agreed to subsidize them to avoid losses to the banks.

Ministry of Finance Measures 117

The procedure for the Ministry of Finance's 44 million yuan loan was originally that the Ministry of Finance would use the Yigeng Indemnity as collateral and issue 44 million yuan in public bonds to the syndicate as a reserve for the syndicate to issue 30 million yuan in securities. Now, the Ministry of Finance hopes to skip the step of the syndicate issuing securities. After the Ministry of Finance issues the securities in the future, it will sell them all to the syndicate. The banks can still use them as cash collateral or for trading, so there will be no risk of financial stagnation. In fact, it is no different from the syndicate issuing them itself. Once the procedures with the syndicate are agreed upon, the Ministry of Finance will soon begin preparations for the issuance.

Increased Taxes on Bund Land; Ministry of Finance Consults Shanghai Municipal Government; Requests Consultation with the Whangpoo Conservancy Board 118

The Ministry of Finance consulted the Shanghai Municipal Government, stating that although the land along the Huangpu River is of the nature of sandy fields and should be handled according to the regulations for sandy fields, the Whangpoo Conservancy Board has reported that all the land owned by the board is reserved for future conservancy or port affairs. Furthermore, most of it is held with licenses issued by the ministry, which is also a fact. Before the conservancy regulations are amended, the city government should consult with the board at any time regarding increasing taxes on Bund land, etc., to avoid disputes.

The Beijing-Guangdong Direct Flight Route Will Open on May 1; Passenger Tickets, Freight, and Mail Will Be Sold and Transported Simultaneously; Two Flights Each Way Between Beijing and Guangdong Every Tuesday and Thursday; New Large Aircraft Purchased Will Not Arrive in China Until February 121

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation's long-planned Beijing-Guangdong flight route has been delayed until now due to problems with the Guangzhou airport. The company has now completed the construction of a new airport at the Shipai Racecourse and has decided to officially open the route on May 1. It will simultaneously carry passengers, freight, and mail, with two flights each way every Tuesday and Thursday. Flight schedules and fares have been set. The large aircraft ordered from Germany will not arrive in China until February. Details are as follows:

Announcement of Opening 122

The company issued an announcement yesterday stating: "Our company's Beijing-Guangdong air route, via Guangzhou, Changsha, Hankou, Luoyang, and Taiyuan to Beijing, is scheduled to open on May 1. Passenger tickets will be sold and freight and mail will be transported from that day. Flights will depart from Beijing and Guangzhou every Tuesday and Thursday, arriving in Guangzhou and Beijing the following afternoon, respectively. It will also connect with our company's existing Shanghai-Xinjiang route in Luoyang and with China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Sichuan route in Hankou. Passengers and merchants traveling to Nanjing, Luoyang, Xi'an, Lanzhou, Beijing, Taiyuan, Hankou, Changsha, or Guangzhou can book directly with our company. Detailed flight schedules and fare charts are available for reference. For mailing services, please contact the post offices."

Flight Schedule 123

The company has decided that the Beijing-Guangdong route will have two flights each way per week. (Southbound flight) Every Tuesday and Thursday at 8:00 AM, it will take off from Beijing and arrive in Luoyang at 2:00 PM for an overnight stay. The next morning at 9:00 AM, it will take off from Luoyang again and arrive in Guangzhou at 6:15 PM on the same day. (Northbound flight) Every Tuesday and Thursday at 7:00 AM, it will take off from Guangzhou and arrive in Luoyang at 4:10 PM on the same day for an overnight stay. The next morning at 8:00 AM, it will take off from Luoyang again and arrive in Beijing at 2:00 PM on the same day. At the same time, it can also connect with the Shanghai-Xinjiang route to Xi'an, Lanzhou, or the various stations in Nanjing and Shanghai.

Passenger Fares 124

The passenger fares for the Beijing-Guangdong route have been decided and calculated based on the measured distance. Beijing to Taiyuan is 450 kilometers, and the fare is 60 yuan. Taiyuan to Luoyang is 350 kilometers, and the fare is 40 yuan. Luoyang to Hankou is 550 kilometers, and the fare is 50 yuan. Hankou to Changsha is 300 kilometers, and the fare is 50 yuan. Changsha to Guangzhou is 600 kilometers, and the fare is 150 yuan. The total distance of the entire route is 2200 kilometers, and the direct fare is 350 yuan.

Sending Personnel for Inspection 125

With the opening of the Beijing-Guangdong route imminent, to ensure the completeness of the stations along the route, the company dispatched engineer He Si on the 21st of this month to depart from Shanghai to Beijing and then inspect the stations in Taiyuan, Luoyang, Hankou, Changsha, Guangzhou, etc., to ensure thoroughness. According to Mr. Li Jingcong, the general manager of the company, speaking to a Xin Xin News Agency reporter, the large JU 52 all-metal aircraft ordered from Germany will not arrive in China until February at the earliest. The rumor that it will arrive in Shanghai within days is not true. Therefore, the Beijing-Guangdong route, which will open on May 1, will temporarily use the existing Junker W 34 aircraft for the flight. Once the new aircraft arrives in Shanghai, it will be replaced.

Shanghai Banking Community Signs Loan Contract for Yu-Ping Railway; Interest Rate of 7.5% Per Annum, Repaid in Five Years; Entire Road Project Scheduled for Completion Within One Year 127

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Yu-Ping Railway, jointly constructed by the governments of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces, is estimated to cost 60 million yuan. It has been decided to first raise half of the amount. The Shanghai banking community has agreed to lend 12 million yuan, and the contract has been signed. The loan guarantee has been approved by the Ministry of Railways and the governing provincial governments. A joint company has been organized to begin construction. Details are reported below:

Total Amount of Capital 128

The Yu-Ping Railway is located between Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces. The importance of the entire road, in terms of military and transportation, is no less than that of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. The governments of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces, in view of this, have planned to open it. Experts have conducted surveys and estimated that the total cost will be 60 million yuan to complete. It was decided to first raise half of the amount to start construction. The authorities of the two provinces each planned to raise 7.7 million yuan. The remaining insufficient funds were borrowed from Shanghai banks. Zeng Yangfu, Xiao Chunjin, and Chen Yaozu, representatives of the Ministry of Railways, were sent to Shanghai to repeatedly negotiate with Zhang Gongquan of the Bank of China, Tang Shoumin of the Bank of Communications, Qian Xinzhi of the Four Banks Savings Association, etc. As a result, it was agreed to lend 12 million yuan.

Contract Signed 129

The contract for the 12 million yuan of capital borrowed from the banking community was formally signed last week. The interest rate was set at 7.5% per annum. The repayment period will begin after the road is completed and will be repaid in installments. It is scheduled to be repaid in full within five years. In addition to the governments of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces using important local tax revenues as collateral, the Ministry of Railways will also use certain bonds as collateral. After the contract was formally signed by both parties, it has been reported to the governing provincial governments for record and approval.

Construction Begins 130

The governments of Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces, having the funds in place, jointly organized the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Joint Company in Beijing. Starting from the 1st of this month, they have hired workers to carry out construction according to the designated route. The first section, from the Yushan Station at the end of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway to Nanchang, is scheduled to be completed by the end of March next year. The second section will be constructed from Nanchang to Pingxiang. The entire project is expected to be completed within two years.

Ministry of Communications: Opening of Shanghai-Shaoxing-Ningbo Long-Distance Telephone Service; Funds of More Than 100,000 Yuan Have Been Raised; Construction Will Begin Within Days and Be Completed in April 135

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the Ministry of Communications, recognizing the busy commercial traffic between Shanghai and Ningbo, decided to open a direct long-distance telephone service between Shanghai and Ningbo to facilitate communication. The Shanghai Municipal Telephone Bureau is responsible for handling this. Funds of more than 100,000 yuan have recently been fully raised, and the work of installing telephone lines is actively underway. It will be formally realized after April. A reporter from the Shenshi News Agency learned the details as follows:

Opening of Shanghai-Ningbo Long-Distance Telephone Service 136

The cities of Shanghai and Ningbo are geographically close, and commercial exchanges are very frequent. In particular, there are more people from Ningbo and Shaoxing residing in Shanghai than from any other region. In order to facilitate communication and foster a closer business relationship between the two regions, the Ministry of Communications has decided to establish a long-distance telephone line connecting Shanghai, Shaoxing, and Ningbo. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau has been specially instructed to handle this project. Following several consultations between the Bureau Chief Mr. Xu Xueyu and the telephone bureaus of Shaoxing and Ningbo, preparations have been actively underway and are now largely completed. The route runs from Shanghai via Hangzhou, then directly to Shaoxing and finally to Ningbo. The Shanghai-Hangzhou section is already in operation. It has recently been decided to construct the Hangzhou-Shaoxing and Shaoxing-Ningbo sections to complete the entire line.

Funding Secured, Completion Expected in April 137

The total cost of constructing the Shanghai-Ningbo long-distance telephone line is estimated to be over ten thousand yuan. Thanks to the support of local gentry and merchants in both Shanghai and Ningbo, the entire amount has now been secured. The survey and construction of the line will commence within days, and the entire project is expected to be completed by April. The detailed regulations for the management and tariffs after the line becomes operational will be drafted by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau and submitted to the Ministry for approval and implementation.

### Chinese National to Compile English-Language China Yearbook, Publication Expected at Year-End 138

Cai Yuanpei, Li Shizeng, Shi Liangcai, Chen Liting, and others have recently initiated the organization of an English-language China Yearbook Society. The society's address is located at 321 Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, Shanghai. Work has already commenced, with the entire book expected to comprise approximately 1.4 million characters. It will adopt the latest compilation methods used in yearbooks from various countries, and the content will strive for brevity and completeness. Experts will be commissioned to write each chapter. The Commercial Press has been tentatively entrusted with publication, with publication scheduled for the end of this year. The Society's editorial rationale has been located and is appended below:

In modern times, yearbooks in various countries can be broadly divided into two categories: those of a specialized nature and those of a general nature. The latter can be further categorized by those focusing on a single country and those focusing on the world. The publication of the Shen Bao Yearbook last year was a huge success, and the first edition is about to be released. Other works of a specialized nature, such as the Economic Yearbook of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Education Yearbook of the Ministry of Education, are also about to be published.

The above works are all in Chinese, which is convenient for Chinese people to reference. However, foreigners wishing to study Chinese issues are unable to consult them due to the significant language barrier. Consider our neighbor Japan, which spends vast sums of money each year to compile and publish an English yearbook to promote its national conditions to the world, regarding it as a powerful tool for international propaganda. The significance of publishing an English yearbook is readily apparent. It is inconceivable that the Chinese have consistently abandoned this important work, allowing an Englishman, Mr. Woodhead, to handle it for more than a decade. This is not only a deficiency in China's cultural publishing industry but also a national disgrace.

Last year, dozens of writers in Shanghai jointly issued a declaration hoping that all national institutions would not provide Mr. Woodhead with materials. However, this is a passive measure. Active work should focus on Chinese people compiling their own English yearbook as a replacement. We, the undersigned, based on this principle, have initiated the organization of an English-language China Yearbook Society, and we hope that the Chinese people will lend their support to this undertaking. We would be very grateful.

Residents of Laoshusha Oppose the Customs' Construction of an Ammunition Depot Four Representatives Petitioned in Beijing, Discussion Held by the Pudong Native Place Association 144

The Jianghai Customs Administration is currently planning to build a large-scale ammunition depot in Laoshusha, Songnan (i.e., Gaoqiaosha). Upon learning of this, the residents of the sandbar became alarmed and immediately convened a meeting of all residents of the sandbar, establishing a People's Self-Defense Corps. After discussion, the residents agreed that the Jianghai Customs' move was deliberately creating difficulties for them, damaging the prosperity of the sandbar, and severely harming the overall plan to revitalize the industry of Laoshusha. They immediately elected Hu Xiong, Chen Fengming, Zhu Yuan, Wang Qisong, Zhang Jintang, and others as representatives to petition in Beijing. Yesterday, a representative from the capital who had returned to Songjiang after filing a lawsuit mentioned this matter, stating (the following is all from the representative's perspective): The Jianghai Customs rented a piece of land that had already been filled in on Laoshusha from the Junpu Bureau, covering an area of approximately one hundred acres. This land is very close to the Asia and other oil depots, and even closer to Guanghua, less than half a li away. It is said that the Jianghai Customs initially submitted a request to the Shanghai Municipal Government for approval, but the Municipal Government refused to approve it because the sandbar had previously been designated by the Municipal Government as an oil depot area with the approval of the Ministries of Industry and Agriculture and Mining. Now, it is attempting to build an ammunition depot on the sandbar, which would be difficult to approve. However, the Jianghai Customs, due to the Municipal Government's disapproval, directly submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance and the Executive Yuan. The Yuan ordered the Shanghai Municipal Government to comply. After receiving the Yuan's order, the Municipal Government, considering the danger posed by the storage of ammunition in the ammunition depot, required the Customs to take responsibility for safety. As a result, the Customs slowly implemented the British government's regulations for the construction of ammunition depots, designating a dangerous zone with a radius of 2,500 feet around the ammunition depot. The Municipal Government issued a joint announcement by the Municipal Land Bureau and the Public Works Bureau, prohibiting people from residing and constructing any buildings within the zone, and declaring that the Customs would not be responsible for any damage within the 2,500 feet. After reading the announcement, the sandbar residents, concerned about the lives and property of all residents of the sandbar, elected Chen Fengming, Zhu Yuan, Hu Xiong, and Wang Qisong as representatives to petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance in Beijing. They were received by Secretary-General Zhao, representing Executive Yuan President Wang, and Vice Minister Qin, representing Ministry of Finance Minister He. In addition to submitting a formal petition, they presented the residents' opinions, arguing that the Jianghai Customs had chosen an inappropriate location because the various oil depots in the area stored huge amounts of gasoline, which was already extremely dangerous. If an ammunition depot was built less than half a li away, the consequences of an explosion would be devastating. Moreover, the oil depot area was prosperous with many merchants and residents, unlike in the past. They earnestly requested the President of the Yuan to revoke the previous order to build an ammunition depot in order to maintain the livelihood of the people. Secretary Zhao and others expressed their care and provided much comfort, promising to instruct the Shanghai Municipal Government to handle the matter properly. The four representatives felt satisfied and returned."

It was also learned that the Pudong Native Place Association held a meeting of directors and supervisors last night, and this case was also discussed. The general consensus was that Laoshusha is located at the northeast corner of Pudong, south of the confluence of the Jiang, Hai, and Pu rivers, at the throat of the transportation gateway. Storing such dangerous goods there would not be safe in peacetime, let alone in the event of an accident. A detailed investigation and study must be carried out, and then suggestions should be made to the authorities for thorough consideration to ensure complete safety.
