Guangzhou Continues to Detain Artificial Silk Interwoven Fabrics The National Goods Maintenance Association Telegraphs Requesting Return 146

The Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association yesterday telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the Guangdong Provincial Government, and the Department of Finance, stating: "We have recently received a letter from the Shanghai Guangbang Silk Fabric United Association stating that Yuyuanxiang, a member of our Association, purchased one hundred bolts of line crepe from the Shanghai Yingfeng Factory Silk Store on behalf of Guangzhou Yutaixiang, and mailed them to Guangzhou on March 5th. The Guangzhou Foreign Goods Piece Goods Special Tax Bureau Zhongxing Company detained them, claiming that they were foreign goods and required payment of a special tax before they could be released. This matter is currently under negotiation. Yesterday, we received a telegram from our counterparts in Guangzhou stating that on the 12th of this month, the company again detained over three thousand bolts of similar goods from various firms. As a result, the firms were forced to temporarily suspend the handling of goods to Shanghai via telegram. It has been found that Zhongxing Company has been in business for many years and has only ever auctioned foreign goods piece goods, never involving domestic goods. Now, they claim that artificial silk interwoven fabrics should be treated as foreign goods. We believe that our country's production is backward, and there is no substitute for artificial silk for the time being. Sometimes, we are forced to use imported raw materials, but if they are processed and manufactured by domestic factories, they are domestic goods. For example, if foreign yarn is used to weave domestic cloth, it conforms to the four classes of domestic goods stipulated in the National Goods Standards promulgated by the Ministry of Industry. How can it be classified as foreign goods? If this continues, the artificial silk interwoven fabric industry will inevitably be destroyed, and the future of domestic goods will be unimaginable. Your Association's business is closely related to ours, and we share the same pain. We hope that you will lend your full support and send telegrams to the relevant authorities in Beijing and Guangdong, as well as to Zhongxing Company, to argue on the basis of reason in order to strengthen our position and achieve the goal of canceling the arbitrary collection of taxes, so as to maintain domestic goods. We would be very grateful." Based on this, we believe that our country's silk fabrics used to sell well at home and abroad, reaching everywhere. However, since the exchange of goods between China and foreign countries, a large number of foreign artificial silk fabrics have been imported and sold in large quantities, and our country's silk fabrics, because of their color and luster, are not as good, and have been abandoned by women, resulting in failure. Silk weaving merchants have carefully studied and followed the methods of Eastern and Western silk, and also used artificial silk to interweave with real silk to form silk, and sold it on the market, so that they can sell well and maintain the status quo. However, since the various countries of the East and West have increased the import tax on our country's silk fabrics, the overseas market for our woven products has lost five or six out of ten. With the loss of Liaoning and Jilin, the only remaining market for silk fabrics has also been seized by strong neighbors. As a result, silk weaving merchants are getting worse year by year and are about to perish. This is the first reason why we urgently hope to find a way to help them get rid of the shackles. The artificial silk used in our country is all imported from the West, and is subject to a heavy tax of about 100% when imported. Weavers have to purchase it and make a living. But East Asian silk fabrics, because of the lack of import tax on artificial silk, are cheap. The South Sea Islands, which used to sell Chinese silk, are now selling East Asian silk. For example, Chinese silk costs one yuan per foot, while East Asian silk costs only five cents per foot. As a result, the South Sea market for Chinese silk has been lost. Fortunately, our National Government is promoting domestic goods, and requires imported silk fabrics to be subject to import tax, so as to maintain the domestic business of domestic goods, which is deeply appreciated by all industrial and commercial circles. If the Zhongxing Company claims that domestic goods are imported and uses its power to detain them, it is illegally destroying domestic goods. Won't the Guangdong market for Chinese silk be lost again? With fewer and fewer silk sales markets, the silk industry is declining day by day. If all the tax bureaus in the country follow suit, our domestic goods industry will inevitably be completely destroyed. Thinking of this, we feel extremely indignant. We should order them to stop and return the detained goods. This is the second reason to get rid of the shackles. The artificial silk in Japan, before it was self-made, was regarded as raw material and not subject to customs duties. After successful manufacturing and large-scale export, it was also not taxed. As a result, Japanese interwoven fabrics were cheaper than the same goods in our country, and could be imported as much as possible and compete in our market. If our country also destroys the slightly defensive fence, it will drive the people of the whole country to use Japanese interwoven fabrics. Isn't this the original intention of the National Government to set up a bureau to collect foreign goods tax? This is the third reason why we should strictly order and warn them not to illegally detain domestic goods. To sum up the three points, the Association believes that what is involved is not only the silk and cloth industries that are affected. Therefore, we dare to perform our duty of maintaining domestic goods and report the situation in detail. We implore your esteemed Yuan to order the Ministry and Department to investigate and verify, and to order the Zhongxing Company to quickly return the detained goods in full and not to have this kind of illegal behavior in the future, so as to maintain the domestic silk and cloth business. We cannot wait for your orders." Respectfully, Wang Jiean, Wang Xingyi, and Wang Hanqiang, Standing Committee Members of the Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association.

Three Dancers at the Lafayette Dance Hall Brawl; Manager's Case Continues Yesterday; Plaintiff Repeatedly Mistakes Manager's Name; Debate Concluded, Verdict Set for the Second of Next Month 150

Dancer Yang Xianmei of the Lafayette Dance Hall, at 3:00 AM on the 9th of this month, inside the hall, was splashed with hot shrimp soup by fellow dancer Pan Meiying, soiling her newly made dance dress, leading to an argument. Another dancer, Chen Aying, assisted Pan in assaulting Yang. Complaining to the manager was not only futile, but she was also reprimanded, insulted, kicked, and injured, and lost her diamond ring and watch. She first went to the Second Special Court for a medical examination, then hired lawyer Huang Xiubo to file a lawsuit against the Lafayette Dance Hall manager and the two dancers, Pan and Chen, accusing them of joint assault in the Second Special District Court, requesting legal investigation.

In addition, she filed a civil suit to recover the lost jewelry and damages of three hundred yuan. Upon receiving the lawsuit, the court held a hearing on the 19th of this month. Because the plaintiff mistakenly listed the name of the first defendant, Lafayette Dance Hall manager Chen Yingjun, as accountant Chen Zhongying, she withdrew the case against Chen Zhongying in court and supplemented the indictment, adding Chen Yingjun and requesting his summons. The court approved this and ordered Pan and Chen to post bail and await rescheduling. These details were previously reported. Yesterday morning, the hearing resumed. Chen Yingjun and the two dancers, Pan and Chen, arrived with their respective defense lawyers. Judge Sun Pengxian presided over the hearing in the Criminal Division Two. First, the defense lawyer of the first defendant, Chen Yingjun, stood up and stated to the court that the name of the first defendant was mistaken in the previous indictment and in this supplementary indictment; the Lafayette Dance Hall manager is actually Chen Yingjun, not Chen Yingjun, and asked the court to note this.

The judge questioned the plaintiff as to who the first defendant actually was. The judge asked the plaintiff, Yang Xianmei, if the person she was accusing was the first defendant present in court. Yang replied that it was him, that he first grabbed her hands and allowed Pan and Chen to slap her face and

arms, and then Chen Yingjun kicked her to the ground. The plaintiff then asked the court to excuse her mistake and requested to correct the name. The judge then questioned Chen Yingjun, who stated that he was 48 years old, from Ningbo, and was the manager of the Lafayette Dance Hall. He said he had not hit the plaintiff. On the morning of April 9, the plaintiff was hitting someone in the writing room. He told her not to hit, but she did not listen. He then said that he would suspend her business tomorrow. Moreover, there were many police officers in the dance hall. If there was a problem, he could call the police, so why would he personally hit her? Later, the plaintiff went to the police station to file a complaint. When he went, he paid her ten yuan to buy clothing material. If it was not enough, he would say more tomorrow. He asked the court to ask the plaintiff if he had given her ten dollars. At this point, Chen Yingjun's defense lawyer stated that there were police officers present at the time and asked that they be summoned to court. The judge then summoned Sun Yuwan, the police officer in charge of the dance hall's entrance. He was first sworn in. He stated that he was managing the cars at the dance hall's main entrance. At that time, he heard a noise inside the hall and entered the writing room, where he saw the plaintiff standing near the writing desk, arguing with the two dancers, Pan and Chen. The manager was sitting in a chair and stood up, telling them not to argue. The plaintiff then went outside. He did not see the plaintiff fall to the ground. Because there were many vehicles in front of the door, he went outside to take care of the vehicles. Later, he saw the plaintiff leave in a Xiang Sheng taxi. The judge then questioned the plaintiff and the defendants, the two dancers Pan and Chen, about the circumstances of the assault. Their statements were the same as recorded in the previous report and will not be repeated here. The judge also asked the plaintiff if there were receipts or evidence for the lost diamond ring and watch. Yang replied that she had purchased them long ago and the receipts had been lost after several moves, but she usually wore them on her hand, and everyone in the hall had seen them. At this point, the court found the facts to be clear and ordered the debate to begin. After mutual debate between the two sides' lawyers, the court announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the verdict for May 2, after which the court adjourned.

Alarming Kerosene Sales in China 152

China spends nearly 10,000,000 yuan annually importing kerosene as a necessary fuel. However, all that is needed in the market is foreign goods. The sales of Mobil and Asiatic in China each year are more than tens of millions. Since the restoration of Sino-Soviet diplomatic relations, the dumping of Russian oil by the Guanghua Company has become a three-way split. Therefore, the import volume of kerosene has increased dramatically compared to before. The statistical quantity of kerosene in the past five years is as follows: 55,177,498 customs taels in 1929; 54,864,540 customs taels in 1930; 64,549,371 customs taels in 1931; 94,244,822 national currency in 1932; and 87,450,738 national currency in 1933.

Increase in Russian Goods Imports 154

Since the restoration of Sino-Soviet diplomatic relations, the Soviet Union has actively shipped its surplus goods to China for dumping. The most notable are gasoline, cement, timber, patterned cloth, and machinery. The dumping of gasoline in China has been dominated by Mobil, Texaco, and Asiatic. Since the dumping of Soviet Russian Guanghua Oil, the prices have been relatively low, and Mobil and the other

three companies have suffered considerable losses. The gasoline market in China has been taken over by Russian oil. As for cement, domestic production is very small, and the market used to use Japanese goods, but now it uses more Russian goods, and domestic cement production has also been severely hit. Soviet

timber has been shipped to China for dumping in recent years, competing fiercely with American goods, and it also has a tendency to monopolize the market. As for patterned cloth, because of its low price, it is quite popular among the Chinese people, with monthly imports reaching about 600,000 yuan. The import of machinery is also showing an upward trend, and it will soon invade the market for dumping.

Red Pill Manufacturing Den Discovered in Dunren Lane, Wangzhi Road; Many Manufacturing Tools Seized on the Spot; Four People Arrested Successively, Mastermind at Large 155

Jin Jiulin, the detective inspector of the Special Agency of the French Concession Police, recently discovered that someone was secretly manufacturing red pills at No. 18, Dunren Lane, Wangzhi Road, a three-story building, late at night, and selling them in the city. The transactions were quite large. On the morning of the day before yesterday, he led detectives Qian Yumin, Zhang Ziying, and officers Liu Dianlong and Cui Zhenguo to secretly search the premises. There was no one in the house. Only in the manufacturing den on the third floor were ten cans of red pills seized, totaling 50,000 pills, one can of raw material white powder, another 92 pounds, one bag of red powder, weighing four pounds, one set of pill-making boards, six lead wire cloth trays, one sieve, one large and one small enameled basin, small basins containing unfinished red wet powder raw materials, five scales, one oven, one plywood board, and six stamps. After the search, it was found that the workers were hiding in No. 13 of the same lane during the day. They immediately rushed there and arrested three women, Lei Liushi (29 years old), Dai Jinzhang (30 years old), and Zhu A'da (44 years old), all from Pudong. Together with the evidence, they were taken to the police station. According to their confessions, the bosses were Sun Peisheng and Zhang Rongqing. Sun worked at the Zhongou Pharmacy at No. 282, Wuma Road in the Public Concession, and Zhang's whereabouts were unknown. The police chief immediately ordered the detention and ordered detective Qian Yumin to go to the Zhongou Pharmacy at 9:00 PM that night, together with detectives from the Public Concession Police, to arrest Sun Peisheng. Zhang, however, had heard the news and escaped, making it impossible to arrest him. Yesterday morning, the French Concession Police escorted the defendants to Criminal Division One of the Second Special District Local Court. Police lawyer Fei Xizhen explained the case and requested a two-week extension to temporarily detain the defendants, pending the police's detailed investigation of the case for prosecution. The evidence was also presented to the court. Subsequently, the police detective reported the discovery of the manufacturing den and the arrest of the defendants. Judge Xiong Huiping reviewed the report and interrogated the defendants. All the defendants denied the charges. The court ordered a rescheduled hearing on May 10 after further investigation. The defendants were returned to custody, and the seized items were stored in the warehouse.

Huamei Launches National Goods Display Competition; Expensive Storefront Windows Offered to the National Goods Industry for Free 156

The China Huamei Tobacco Company held the "Buy Si Gan" scholarship last year, which was praised by all sectors of society. The company will now establish a storefront on Nanjing Road. It is heard that at the beginning of the opening, it will launch the "Huamei National Goods Storefront Display Competition" to commemorate the event. Its purpose is threefold: (1) to establish a spirit of mutual assistance among national goods factories, (2) to promote the exquisiteness of national goods factory products, and (3) to promote the art of storefront display advertising. This kind of contribution that is beneficial to the national goods industry is worthy of our praise. The methods are recorded as follows: (1) The company's large storefront windows on Nanjing Road, two in total, will be offered free of charge to the national goods industry for the purpose of this "Huamei" National Goods Storefront Display Competition. (2) This competition will last for one year from the opening to the closing date. The opening date will be announced separately. (3) All factory members of the Ministry of Industry and any national goods association in Shanghai are eligible to participate in the competition. (4) National goods factories participating in the competition are limited to displaying their own factory products and must first fill out a registration form with the company's competition department. (5) The display competition period for each factory is limited to ten days from the date of display, with the order determined by the order of registration. (6) The selection standards for the display competition are threefold: (1) the loftiness of the meaning, (2) the exquisiteness of the design, and (3) the harmony of the colors. (7) The display style is planned by the factory itself, but it must be approved by the company before the display. (8) The company will invite art experts to evaluate the entries based on the competition selection standards and determine the rankings. (9) The company has prepared ten commemorative cups to be awarded to the designers of the top ten factories to increase interest. (10) During the display period of each factory, the company can also provide free distribution of promotional materials and samples for the company. (11) The company will take photos of each display style, collect them together, and compile them into a commemorative album at the closing of the competition, which will be distributed to all sectors of society. (12) Factories participating in the competition that need to add commemorative albums for promotional purposes can calculate the cost at the company's cost.

Pirated A Laughterful Marriage Discovered on the Market; Everything is the Same as the Real One, but the Printing is Inferior; The Book Also Contains Signatures by Li Haoran and Wang Xishen - Police Prosecute on Two Charges 157

Zhang Henshui's novel A Laughterful Marriage has been popular since its publication and has been reprinted many times. The copyright was acquired by the Sanyou Bookstore on Fuzhou Road, and a registration certificate No. 660 was issued by the Ministry of Interior. Li Zengyao, the manager of Sanyou Bookstore, learned that the Chunming Bookstore at No. 440 Fuzhou Road was selling pirated copies of A Laughterful Marriage and the book Zibian published by the company. On the 4th of this month, he ordered his partners Yan Changyan and Zhang Hongdao to purchase three copies of A Laughterful Marriage and five copies of Zibian from Chunming, costing 3.9 yuan. Chunming did not store the books in the store but ordered its partners to retrieve them from the Wenguang Bookstore at No. 3, Lane 62, Shandong Road. After Yan and Zhang purchased the counterfeit books, they took them back and handed them over to Li. On the morning of the 14th, Li reported to the Laozha Police Station, requesting an investigation. Chinese detective Zhang Yuanqing and detective Xu Zexin purchased five copies of A Laughterful Marriage and other books from Chunming for 12 yuan (all with secret marks), while Zibian was not purchased at the time. The detectives took the books back and, after examining them, saw that the pirated A Laughterful Marriage looked the same as the real one, but the printing was blurry and inferior. They immediately went to arrest Chen Zhaochun, the manager of Chunming, a native of Haimen, and took him back to the police station. They also went to the Wenguang Bookstore to search, but found nothing. Chen Zhaohuan, the manager of Wenguang, confessed that the pirated Zibian was printed by the Qizhi Printing House at No. 19, Lane 53, Ximen Road, French Concession. The detectives went to the printing house and seized the printing plates and took them back to the police station. Chen Zhaochun confessed that he had purchased 128 copies of A Laughterful Marriage from Ping Jinya of the Zhongyang Bookstore at No. 6, Lane 328, Fuzhou Road for 64 yuan on February 12 of this year, after being mentioned by his shop assistant Zhang Boyin. The detectives went to the Zhongyang Bookstore to investigate, but Ping Jinya absolutely denied it. At that time, the police released Chen after filing a report and requesting the First Special Court to issue a subpoena. Yesterday morning, Chen was summoned to Criminal Division Two of the First Special Court. Judge Deng Baosun opened the court and heard the above situation from police lawyer Qian Xunjiu. He stated that he was now prosecuting according to Article 269 of the Criminal Law, and because the book had signatures and inscriptions by Li Haoran and Wang Xishen, all stamped with seals, he believed that there was also a situation of counterfeiting private seals, and prosecuted according to Articles 234 and 44 of the Criminal Law. He also stated that the case of the pirated Zibian has been prosecuted separately. Subsequently, Chinese detective Zhang Yuanqing and detective Xu Zexin submitted a report on the investigation. When Chen Zhaochun was questioned, he stated that he had purchased the novel A Laughterful Marriage at the door on February 12, reversing his previous statement at the police station that he had purchased it from the Zhongyang Bookstore. The judge asked him why his testimony in court was inconsistent with his testimony at the police station. He replied that he was wary at the police station. When asked if he had been tortured, he replied no. The judge said that since there was no torture, the police's statement was difficult to overturn. Judge Deng then said that since the police had already prosecuted the Zibian case separately, it was necessary to review whether there was any connection and whether it should be tried together, and ordered that the case be rescheduled for the 28th for further hearing. The defendant Chen Zhaochun was ordered to pay a shop guarantee of 1,000 yuan.

Abduction No Different from Kidnapping; The "Small Collapsed Cake" Good Deed Has Many Twists; Eight Characters Written on a Cigarette Pack 158

Liu Yunxian, a doctor at No. 53, Dajing Road in the city, married a woman surnamed Xu from Huzhou. Xu has a younger sister, Yunzhen, who is 18 years old, petite and exquisite, with a good appearance, and still unmarried. Because her family was poor, her mother asked her eldest daughter to bring her to Shanghai to find work, and she temporarily resided at Liu Yunxian's home. Unexpectedly, she was recently seen by a "Baixiang Ren" (a person who loafs around doing nothing) in the French Concession nicknamed "Small Collapsed Cake," who wanted to marry Xu Yunzhen. He had personally gone to Liu Xu's home in the city to propose marriage and asked about Yunzhen's age, recording it on a cigarette pack, and volunteered to pay 60 yuan for the tea ceremony and two gold rings as betrothal gifts. At that time, Ms. Xu replied that this marriage matter must be approved by Yunzhen's mother, who was currently in the countryside, and that she would wait to write a letter to seek her consent before making a decision. Unexpectedly, after several days, the "Baixiang Ren" "Small Collapsed Cake" acted arbitrarily, deciding to marry her alone yesterday and leading several hooligans to hire a rickshaw. At 11:00 AM yesterday, they went to Liu Yunxian's home on Dajing Road and forcibly pushed Xu Yunzhen onto the rickshaw and carried her to a certain hotel in the French Concession. At that time, Mr. and Mrs. Liu Yunxian were not at home. When Ms. Liu Xu returned home and learned that "Small Collapsed Cake" had forcibly abducted her, which was no different from kidnapping, she followed her to the French Concession and reported to the Songshan Road Police Station. The police arrested "Small Collapsed Cake" and Liu Yunzhen together. According to Ms. Liu Xu, they had only talked about the marriage for a few days, and she had not agreed, so how could he forcibly abduct her? She requested punishment. According to "Small Collapsed Cake," he had already paid 60 yuan in betrothal gifts and presented the eight characters for Liu Yunzhen's age written on the cigarette pack as proof that the other party had provided them. Now they were reneging on the marriage, and he requested compensation for all losses. After questioning, the police chief found that both parties were at fault. Liu Yunzhen was still under the custody of Liu Xu, and they were ordered to sue each other in court.

Impostor Masquerades as Lawyer Ma Junshuo, Advertising for a Clerk; More than a Hundred Applicants; Lawyer Ma Declares It Is Not True - The Ring Leader He Jisheng is Repeatedly Disturbed and Arrested 159

Lawyer Ma Junshuo, from Nantong, lives at No. 81, Liulin Villa, Yuyuan Road, and has an office at No. 405, Mainland Commercial Field. On the 20th of this month, in the advertisement column of a certain newspaper, there was suddenly an advertisement for a lawyer hiring a clerk, the content of which was roughly as follows: "A certain lawyer now intends to hire two clerks, with a monthly salary of 50 yuan, including room and board, regardless of gender or qualifications, as long as they are fluent in Chinese and can write in small regular script. Applicants should come to No. 81, Liulin Villa, Yuyuan Road, between 7:00 AM and 9:00 AM every day for an interview." Since the advertisement was published, dozens of people went to apply that day. At that time, lawyer Ma did not know that someone was secretly playing tricks. After being reported, he inquired with the applicants and learned the truth, and then declared to each applicant that it was not true and dispersed them. On the one hand, he reported to the General Patrol Room and the Jing'an Temple Patrol Room, requesting an investigation. On the other hand, Ma Junshuo published a statement in the newspaper. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 21st, people still went to Ma's door, and there were even more than the previous day, reaching more than a hundred men and women. Among them, one person in charge, named He Jisheng (He Shiping), 34 years old, from Shaoxing, who was a doctor at the Postal Workers' Union, knocked on the door and entered, wanting to see lawyer Ma. Ma's younger sister, Ma Shuxian, met him instead. When asked about the purpose of the application, he replied that this matter was a trick by a villain and was not true. The people then withdrew, but in recent days, He has gone to Ma's residence and office to harass him, claiming that he has suffered considerable losses because of this matter. Moreover, the day of the application happened to be a heavy rain, and his clothes were soaked and the round-trip fare was not small. Lawyer Ma should be responsible for compensation, otherwise there will be considerable means to deal with him. The words were threatening and bordering on extortion. Ma then reported to the police again, and Detective Wang Yubin secretly investigated. The afternoon before yesterday, He Jisheng went to Ma's office again and was arrested by Detective Wang and taken to the Jing'an Temple Patrol Room for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to Criminal Division Eight of the First Special Court. The police prosecuted He Jisheng according to Article 370, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law for attempted extortion by intimidation. Then, Kungpuchi lawyer Gan Jingxian claimed that after the police received Ma Junshuo's report on April 20, they went to the newspaper office to investigate. According to reports, the advertisement was sent by the Nanyang Advertising Agency on Fuzhou Road. The detectives then went to Nanyang to inquire and presented a draft paper with the seal of lawyer Ma Junshuo. Now, Ma has identified that the seal is actually forged. The defendant in this case has repeatedly gone to Ma's home and office to see Ma Junshuo, and was met by clerk Chen Yaozu. According to the defendant's

statement, he had suffered losses because Ma had advertised for a clerk

and Ma should compensate him, and he often pressed him by telephone. Ma reported to the police, who sent detectives to arrest the defendant. Now, because the investigation of this case needs to continue, it is requested that it be approved to be rescheduled. Subsequently, Ma Junshuo complained about the above situation, and said that he had recently not offended anyone and that he did not know the defendant at all. Furthermore, Ma Shuxian, Ma Junshuo's sister, testified that the defendant had repeatedly come to the house to find her brother, and I met him instead. When asked what he was doing there, he hesitated and also referred to me as Miss Li, I don't know why. When He Jisheng, the defendant, was interrogated, he claimed that he was a volunteer doctor at the Postal Workers' Union. Because his income was small, he was happy to go to apply after seeing the newspaper advertising for Ma Lawyer to hire a clerk with a monthly salary of fifty yuan. When he arrived, he saw many people surrounding Ma's door. He knocked on the door and entered to ask. Miss Ma said that it was not true. I then returned. Yesterday afternoon, I went to Ma Lawyer's office alone, intending to ask Ma to find a position as a public relations officer, which is why I was arrested. There was no act of fraud. After Liu Yugui, the judge, compared the defendant's handwriting in court, he recognized that the handwriting on the forged original draft of the clerk recruitment and the names on the fabricated wedding invitation were entirely his own handwriting. He then ordered that the trial be rescheduled for seven days and the defendant was sent back to custody.

Liu said not to be sad, take care of the two children, it is best if you can maintain your chastity, and kissed the two children once. Judge Shen then ordered the six prisoners to be sent to the Shanghai Local Court Procuratorate for execution according to law. Chinese and Western detectives from the police station escorted the six men, along with their case files and photos, to the Caohejing Second Prison execution ground in a car. firing squad.

Dumping of Japanese Calcium Carbonate in China 161

The New Sound Agency reports that China's industrial chemical calcium carbonate has long relied on supplies from foreign merchants in Japan, the United States, and Germany. Later, Chinese companies and manufacturers producing calcium carbonate were established in Shanghai, including Da Zhonghua Xinye and Zhao Xin. Therefore, the raw materials used by factories such as Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory are supplied by Da Zhonghua. However, other manufacturers still use foreign goods due to their lower prices. According to industrial sources, the Shanghai calcium carbonate market is currently expanding with significant Japanese trade influence. American and German products, though of high quality, are expensive, leading to slow sales. Chinese products are not inferior to those from the US and Germany, but the Japanese are using dumping strategies to suppress us. Last spring, prices ranged between four and five yuan, but this year, due to competitive dumping, they have fallen to two yuan four jiao to three yuan five jiao. Recently, it was also heard that a batch had arrived in Shanghai from a certain Japanese import ship.

Yu Junsong's Lawsuit and Verdict: Second Trial Finds Him Not Guilty 162

Local obstetrician Yu Junsong was sued by lawyer Tian Heming last year and was found not guilty by the Shanghai First Special District Court. Tian appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court, which also found Yu Junsong not guilty and dismissed the appeal. The Second Branch of the High Court's Criminal Judgment No. 469 was issued yesterday. The key points are as follows: Appellant: Tian Heming, Agent Lawyer: Huang Yingrong, Defendant: Yu Junsong, Defense Lawyer: Jiang Yiping. The above-listed appellant filed an appeal against the first instance judgment of the Shanghai First Special District Court on January 16, 1934, in a case involving the defendant's negligence leading to death. The court's judgment is as follows: (Verdict) Appeal dismissed. (Reason) It is undisputed by both parties that the appellant's wife, Gu Liyi, died of dysentery after childbirth, and the cause was both amoebic and bacillary dysentery. The only point to be investigated is whether the defendant knew it was bacillary dysentery and whether he treated it according to the treatment for bacillary dysentery. According to the defendant, on August 4, 1933, Gu Liyi had diarrhea and a high fever. Her stool was sent to Zhu Yanggao for microscopic examination, and amoebae were found. In addition to injecting emetine for amoebic dysentery, he also injected 20 cc of serum for bacillary dysentery. On the 5th, Zhu Yanggao reported that there was bacillary dysentery and suggested injecting 20 cc of serum, citing report No. 4092 as evidence. Therefore, the appellant's argument that the defendant never knew there was bacillary dysentery is unfounded. Even if the serum injection on the 4th was before Zhu Yanggao's report, it is common for a doctor to suspect bacillary dysentery based on experience and observation and to try an injection first to observe the reaction. As for the claim that Zhu Yanggao's report No. 4092 was forged, the Forensic Institute has identified it as having been torn from the same stub number and not added later. Zhu Yanggao also explained in court that the minus sign on the form and the different signature pointed out in the鉴定书 were due to the use of stub No. 4088, which was the stool sent on the 4th, for cultivation, hence the two lines indicating no check, and the latter was due to carelessness. He cited stub numbers 3372 and 3385 as evidence to show that he had signed like this before. The examination of No. 4092 used stool from No. 4088 for cultivation and was not related to No. 4091. Therefore, Zhu Yanggao's report is not questionable. However, the appellant also claimed that no serum injections were given on the 6th and 7th, which was inappropriate. According to the defendant, the appellant thought the serum was too expensive and did not want to inject it, as evidenced by Qiu Lizhen's statement about how the appellant prevented the serum injection, and Zhang Baoying's statement that on the 8th, when she was discharged from the hospital, the appellant said that Dr. Yu had ruined the injection. Tao Chengfan said that on the 7th, while visiting the patient, he heard two parties arguing, one wanting an injection and the other refusing, and after the dispute, the doctor told him that he was a lawyer. Furthermore, the appellant admitted in the first trial that on the 4th and 5th, the defendant wanted to inject serum, but he thought it was fraud because it had not been tested on the 4th, so how could he know there was a need to inject serum. For ordinary dysentery, there is amoeba, so emetine can be injected, and the appellant bought the serum himself and returned it to the hospital. Therefore, the defendant's statement that the appellant did not want to inject because it was too expensive is not false. As a result, the defendant, in response to the court's question of why he did not force him or ask him to leave the hospital, replied, "I talked to him, and he said that as a lawyer, what he said is always the law, and I have no way." This is also the truth. The appellant's intention to blame the defendant is unreasonable. According to Article 384 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the judgment is released. April 18, 1934, Criminal Division of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Presiding Judge: Yu Hua, Judge: Zhao Zheng鏜, Judge: Zhou Han. This document is certified as identical to the original. Clerk: Shen.

Tea Industry to Use New Weights and Measures: Production and Sales Parties Decide on Implementation Methods, Effective May 1st 163

The Mao Tea Industry Association, after receiving the Ministry's new weights and measures system, has repeatedly convened meetings to discuss specific methods. Due to long-standing customs, a sudden change is causing difficulties in business implementation procedures. The association felt that procrastination was inappropriate, so after repeated discussions and compromises with both production and sales parties, it was decided to implement the new system starting May 1st. For the production side, the settlement will be calculated by converting the old scales at a rate of 77.7%, and for the buying side, the settlement will be based on 80% of the market scale. The association has reported this to the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for record.

Goods Shipped to the Philippines Must Not Be Packed with Rice Straw: Announcement by the US Consulate General 171

The US Consulate General in Shanghai issued an announcement that all goods shipped to the Philippines must not be packed with rice straw or secured with rice husks. Violators will be fined 1,000 pesos (Philippine currency) and the original goods will be returned to the place of export to prevent the spread of rice weevils into the Philippines.

Report on the association's affairs and economic situation over the past year. B. Discussion: (1) Case on the collection of annual membership fees, resolved to collect according to three levels. (2) Case on purchasing yellow coloring produced by an improved tea coloring factory, resolved to pass. (3) Case on the fact that yellow coloring left over from last year cannot be used in accordance with the Commodity Inspection Bureau's ban and should be returned to the improved tea coloring factory, resolved to pass. (8) Committee member Peng proposed that the association's rent should be tentatively set at ten yuan per month, resolved to proceed accordingly. (9) Committee member Peng proposed that the new tea season is approaching and France has increased import tariffs, so it is appropriate to purchase goods at low mountain prices and not set high prices in order to reduce collection costs, resolved to pass.

Publishing World 185

Publication of "Answers to Questions on Stamp Tax." The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to various trade associations stating: "Stamp tax is a good tax recognized by all countries. Paying it according to law is the duty of every citizen. However, merchants, not understanding the meaning of the regulations, sometimes affix stamps incorrectly on account books and documents, resulting in severe penalties. Those discussing this find it troubling. The Chamber has therefore collected common questions about stamp duty encountered in commerce and compiled them into a book, "Answers to Questions on Stamp Tax," divided into fifteen categories, totaling over eighty items. It contains detailed explanations of unfair penalties and appeal procedures, providing a practical reference for businesses regarding stamp duty payment. The price is fifteen cents per copy. It is hoped that you will notify your members to purchase them directly."

Reading Q&A

How to Collect and Discern International News (3) 190

Over the past two days, some principles for discerning international news have been briefly introduced. Today, I will continue to offer principles and briefly touch on how to read magazines, editorials, etc. - Editor

Fourth, understand the exploratory function of news. For example, before the Manchurian puppet state changed its system, Japan deliberately released many [rumors] to test the international atmosphere. Recently, Japan, wanting to further invade China, specifically released a statement on April 17th by the Japanese Foreign Ministry to the great powers [prohibiting interference in China]. Both are using news as a diplomatic precursor. Naturally, after the exploration, if it does not encounter a major blow, then direct action follows. Otherwise, it may temporarily ease up and switch to another policy. Exploration plays a significant role when diplomacy encounters major setbacks. At this time, news released by news agencies often deliberately spreads an optimistic atmosphere to ease diplomatic difficulties. In short, a country's news always closely echoes its diplomatic policy, and exploration is mostly used during periods of hesitation in diplomatic proceedings. Therefore, we should not regard [exploration] as merely [exploration] but also pay attention to the development of the news.

Fifth, the so-called development of news refers to the process of an international event, which is often overlooked by newspaper readers. In Chinese newspapers, because of the lack of systematic discussions, this difficulty is especially felt. We should pay attention to the time of news releases in daily newspapers and the many news items related before and after this news. We should not treat each day's news as fixed but seek to understand a news item in its context. Regarding this point, daily newspapers often fail to meet the readers' expectations. Daily newspapers themselves naturally know this is a deficiency. The remedy is mostly to include [foreign dispatches], such as the Shen Bao's [foreign dispatches], Xinwen Bao, and Min Bao's [European dispatches], or to publish a [weekly intelligence] or write a more systematic monograph or editorial to provide readers with systematic knowledge. Therefore, these dispatches, essays, and commentaries should be read carefully.

Sixth, and lastly, it should be noted that the news printed in newspapers of various countries rarely has absolute objective independence. It always undergoes some consideration and modification to suit its own political views and foreign policy. Even if it is not a government-run newspaper, it still cannot publish news that violates the fundamental principles of the country. Therefore, readers should not assume that everything published by private newspapers is completely reliable. For example, Reuters will never publish that Tibetan soldiers invaded the rear of the British Empire, and Havas will not point out that the Nine Small Islands indeed belong to China. Rengo and Shimbun Rengo will not regard the Japanese Foreign Ministry's statement on April 17th as a Japanese conspiracy to monopolize China. Not only them, but even private British, French, and Japanese newspapers, which usually boast of their objective stance and no political backing, dare not do so. Everything is related to politics. Newspapers now are especially a political tool and cannot have supra-political international news. Even if some news is indeed true in itself but does not cater to the rulers and suddenly takes a unique stance, it must represent a kind of politics. Therefore, international researchers standing in an objective position, if they want to clarify right and wrong, should first wash away some of the added things from the upper layers for each international event.

Seventh, do not neglect the newspapers' records of the words and actions of political figures. A short message can sometimes contain great significance. Roosevelt's national policy is often decided on yachts, and Herriot also likes to travel, having visited Spain and Moscow, which improved Franco-Soviet relations. Other international exchanges, such as politicians being sick, wealthy people hosting guests, royal marriages, art expositions, tour groups, sightseeing teams, exchange professors, etc., are sometimes particularly noteworthy. As for Semenov (leader of the White Russians) running from Japan to Harbin and Litvinov going from Moscow to Washington, they have extraordinary significance.

In addition, I must provide some tips on magazines, essays, editorials, and the like.

Generally, these things have a certain system when discussing an international event, making it easier to obtain an overview of an event compared to reading a daily newspaper. However, these things are always several days or several dozens of days slower than telegrams and cannot be as fast as daily newspapers. Needless to say, these things are essential reading for those who study international issues. But the propaganda effect of these things is also stronger than a telegram or several news items. Readers are easily captivated by them. All of these things are political, consciously promoting a certain political position. When selecting this part of the material, it is best to also select the opposing views for comparison. Readers should especially pay attention to the background of such publications and the party affiliations of the authors.

In short, the observation of international news often involves inference from the opposite, side, or before and after, rather than directly looking at the front. Therefore, under the current system, everything must be understood in contradictions, and one cannot listen to only one side's opinion. The most important thing to pay attention to is that everything must be understood as a process, finding the main clues that promote the international situation.

The above points are merely things that the editor has written off the cuff. Naturally, the methods of distinguishing international news are not limited to this. But if intelligent readers can fully apply the above points, it would be quite impressive. Distinguishing the truth or falsehood of news is not a technical problem but requires some academic training. Therefore, I hope readers will not neglect the study of the most basic theories of social science.

We hope to have other opportunities soon to discuss this issue in detail further. (End)

Education News: External Ministry of Education Inspection: A Record of the Return Visit to Beijing by Higher Education Personnel: The Ministry of Education has had a consistent policy of reorganization in recent years for higher education, striving for improvement. This time, it dispatched six commissioners (plus Hao Gengsheng, a supervisor inspecting physical education) to various provinces and cities to inspect public and private colleges and universities. This is the first time since the establishment of the Republic of China. Previously, when Ren Hongjun was in charge of the Higher Education Department of the former Beijing Ministry of Education, he intended to conduct inspections of higher education, and a committee had already been organized, but it never materialized. Since the departure of the ministry's dispatched inspectors, their movements have been repeatedly reported in newspapers throughout the country. Now, nearly two months later, the commissioners have completed their missions. Sun, Guo, Chen, and Liu, who returned to Beijing last, reported to the ministry on the 25th. Upon hearing the news, the reporter made a special trip to inquire about the inspection. They were received, and a summary of the situation is recorded below.

Inspection Personnel: The general inspection team consisted of Chen Kezhong, Sun Guofeng, Liu Yingshi, and Guo Youshou. Hao Gengsheng specialized in inspecting physical education (Jinan and Qingdao were not visited). Zhou Tianfang also participated in the inspection of Beijing and Tianjin. Pang Jingzhou was responsible for inspecting medicine. Chen Kezhong is the director of the Natural Science Group of the National Compilation and Translation Bureau, and Liu Yingshi is the chief editor of Book Review. Sun Guofeng, Guo Youshou, and Zhou Tianfang are all specialists in the Ministry of Education. Hao Gengsheng is a physical education supervisor for the Ministry of Education, and Pang Jingzhou is a famous doctor in Shanghai who once served as the president of Tongde Medical School (specializing in inspecting medical colleges and medical vocational schools). Liu, Guo, Chen, and Sun are natives of Jiangsu, Sichuan, Fujian, and Liaoning provinces, respectively, which is a coincidence, representing the four directions: east, west, south, and north.

Inspection Locations: Six provinces, including Shandong, Hebei, Henan, Hunan, Hubei, and Anhui, as well as three cities, Qingdao, Tianjin, and Beijing, were within the scope of the inspection. They departed from Beijing on March 6th. As of today, out of the 52 days, excluding the national mourning for Sun Yat-sen and the memorial day of Huanghuagang and seven Sundays, and seven days of spring break, there were 36 days available for inspection work. A portion of these 36 days was spent traveling. The journey took eight days and six nights, plus five and a half days. Pang Jingzhou went south after going to Baoding, then Kaifeng from Jinan to Beijing.

Schools Inspected: The schools inspected were public and private colleges and universities. In terms of nature, public schools can be divided into national and provincial categories, while private schools are divided into registered and unregistered categories. (A) [National Universities, Colleges, and Vocational Schools]: Shandong University, Peking University, Peiping University, Normal University, Tsinghua University, Wuhan University, Beiyang Institute of Technology, Preparatory Office of the Peiping Art Vocational School. (B) [Provincial Universities, Colleges, and Vocational Schools]: Northeast University, Henan University, Hunan University, Anhui University, Hebei Institute of Technology, Hebei Women's Normal College, Hebei College of Law and Commerce, Hebei Agricultural College, Hebei Medical College, Hubei Provincial College of Education, Shandong Provincial Medical Vocational School, Hebei Provincial Fisheries Vocational School, Henan Water Conservancy Engineering Vocational School. (C) [Registered Private Universities, Colleges, and Vocational Schools]: Qilu University, Nankai University, Sino-French University, Fu Jen Catholic University, Yenching University, Huazhong University, Zhonghua University, Peking Union Medical College, Tianjin Institute of Commerce and Industry, China College, Chaoyang College, Xiangya Medical College, Peiping Railway College, (Provisionally Approved) Republic of China College, (Provisionally Approved) Boone Library School, Wuchang Art Vocational School. (D) [Closed and Unregistered Schools]: North China College, Duwen College, Pingmin College, (Closed) Confucius College, (Largely Closed) Jinghua Academy of Fine Arts, Peiping United Art Academy, Peiping Art Vocational School, Peiping Art School, Women's Western Painting School, Advanced French College, College of Finance and Commerce, Qunzhi College of Political Science and Law, Drama Vocational School. In total, eight national schools, thirteen provincial schools, sixteen registered private schools, and thirteen closed and unregistered schools were inspected, totaling fifty schools.

Scope of Inspection: In addition to the specific issues that the Ministry of Education instructed to investigate at each school, the general scope of inspection included the following items: (A) In terms of administration, matters related to general affairs, academic affairs, accounting, and registration were included. In accounting, the focus was on whether the actual expenditure and distribution of funds were reasonable. In registration, the focus was on whether admission and term examinations were strict, the statistics of faculty and student absences, and their handling methods. For private schools, deposit slips for the foundation were also reviewed. (B) In terms of equipment, items such as libraries, laboratories, workshops, farms, and instruments and medicines of various science, engineering, and agriculture colleges were included. The focus was on whether the equipment was in line with actual needs. (C) In terms of teaching, in addition to visiting classrooms to observe lectures, special attention was paid to the content of teaching materials and student notes. (D) In terms of performance evaluation, in addition to reviewing entrance and term exam papers and experimental reports, special attention was paid to whether the thesis topics of science, engineering, and agriculture colleges were in line with the needs of the country and the local area.

Ministry of Education Orders Elementary and Middle Schools to Emphasize Arithmetic and Natural Sciences: Cannot Recite Literary Chinese or Add English and Japanese: (Nanjing, 26th) The Ministry of Education ordered the education departments of all provinces and cities: Recently, it has been found that some local junior high schools and elementary schools designate classics and force students to recite them, and some elementary schools recite literary Chinese or add old subjects such as English and Japanese. This not only violates the regulations and curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools promulgated by the Ministry, but also increases the burden on students, causing the performance in arithmetic and natural sciences to decline. (According to reports from various provinces and cities, the results of local joint examinations show that the performance in arithmetic and natural sciences is the worst). This is very wrong. It is hereby ordered that the departments instruct their subordinate public and private middle schools and inform the affiliated primary and secondary schools of national universities in the region to comply with laws and regulations in all course subjects and the content of Chinese and national language. Superintendents are responsible for strict supervision. If the above situation is found, it should be corrected immediately. Comply immediately.

Ministry of Education Formulates Standard Equipment for Middle School Science and Chemistry: (Nanjing, 26th) The Ministry of Education formulated standards for physics equipment and chemistry equipment for middle schools, which were announced on the 26th.

Ministry of Education Plans to Prohibit Students from Smoking Cigarettes: (Nanjing, 26th) The Ministry of Education plans to order the education departments of all provinces and cities to instruct their subordinate schools to strictly prohibit students from smoking cigarettes.

To date, 4,386.93 yuan of arrears have been cleared, and 34,887.347 yuan of principal and interest on the transferred loans have been repaid. The remaining arrears will be cleared according to the department's order. The funds for this semester are insufficient by nearly 30,000 yuan due to the use of income from the previous semester to repay the transferred loans and clear arrears, totaling nearly 40,000 yuan. A plan has been drafted and submitted to the county government meeting for approval, and it is expected that funds can be distributed monthly and on time, so that arrears will not occur again. The Jiangsu Education Department Dispatches Personnel to Inspect Secondary Education Throughout the Province: Zhou Yigeng and Others Arrive in Shanghai from Nantong: In order to understand the current situation of secondary education in Jiangsu Province and improve it, the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department dispatched personnel to various counties and cities on the 20th of this month for inspection. Yesterday, Zhou Yigeng, Jin Chongru, and Xie Weidong arrived in Shanghai from Nantong. According to Mr. Zhou, Nantong has always been known as a model for handicrafts. Since Zhang Jian's death, the area has lacked a leading figure for unified leadership. In addition, the Nantong cloth woven on wooden looms, which used to be sold outside the customs, is now in danger of bankruptcy due to the interruption of sales. Social, economic, and educational conditions, which are interrelated, are also deteriorating. However, the 13 provincial secondary schools in the area are still able to maintain the status quo, and the annual income and expenditure are balanced. Management is strict, equipment is considered perfect, and students have a lot of extracurricular activities, especially physical education, which has developed more than in previous years. The three of us are only inspecting secondary schools. Other normal schools have special commissioners. We will transfer to Suzhou for inspection soon and then return to the province to report. The improvement plan is not convenient to publish yet.

The Municipal Education Bureau Held the Second Public Speech of the Year Yesterday: At Wu Ben Girls' High School, Mr. Dong Renjian Gave a Speech on Civic Training and the New Life Movement: The Municipal Education Bureau held the second public speech of the year at Wu Ben Girls' High School yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. Mr. Dong Renjian, a professor at Great China University, gave a speech entitled "Civic Training and the New Life Movement." Over 500 teachers from various schools attended. An excerpt of his speech is as follows: (1) What is a citizen? In terms of book definition, public is the opposite of private, so a citizen is not a private person. When a person is born, there is no concept of public. As he grows up, he becomes socialized, humanized, or grouped with parents, family, school, and even the social body. Therefore, a citizen can be said not to be a private person, but purely socialized. (2) What is training? Training and education are often used interchangeably, but training is a mechanical, action-oriented habit without thought. It teaches people how and what to do, while education is thoughtful. It not only teaches people how and what to do, but also teaches people why. However, the training in civic training is definitely not animal training. (3) What is new life? Life itself is neither new nor old, and there is no absolute newness or absolute oldness. Therefore, the new life is just a transformation of the old life. (4) What is a movement? There are two types of movements: one is propaganda-oriented, and the other is education-oriented. The movement of the New Life Movement is not only propaganda but also educational work. Civic training and the New Life Movement have the same goals and methods. The goal is education, and the method is transformation. Therefore, civic training is the New Life Movement, and the New Life Movement is civic training. Its starting point is in elementary school. Neither is book knowledge, nor is it animal training, nor is it a moral lesson, nor is it sectarian propaganda. Its implementation principle is, first, to make children understand what the current moral standards of society are; second, to make them realize it; and third, to help them so that they have no difficulties.

Special Issue: Tong Xingbai Speaks on the Problem of Knowing and Doing in the New Life Movement (II) by Chen Dongbai: In Chinese history, from the Zhou and Qin dynasties to a hundred years ago, in this long period of two thousand years, the lifestyle of society was originally very disciplined and very restrained. There is no need to talk about the spiritual aspect. Even in the four aspects of clothing, food, housing, and transportation, the ancients paid more attention to it than we do today when we talk about the new life. For clothing, not only was it neat, clean, simple, and plain, but also the quality, color, and manufacturing method of the clothes had to be divided into grades, either based on titles, such as the emperor's clothes, the minister's clothes, and the people's clothes, or based on ceremonies, such as court clothes, sacrificial clothes, wedding clothes, and mourning clothes. The strictness of the rules is hard to describe in a word. Mencius said, "Those who are fifty years old can wear silk clothes." It can be seen that there was still a distinction between age and material. As for food, what we talk about in the new life is cleanliness, simplicity, and hygiene, but the ancients were not only like this, but also had a way of eating and etiquette of eating, without any difference. Confucius can be regarded as the standard figure of China. Later generations regarded him as typical, but Confucius was very particular about eating and drinking. "He would not sit if the mat was not straight" and "He would not eat if the meat was not cut properly." Even not eating at the wrong time, not eating overnight, and not eating rotten food can already show the strictness of one aspect. The same is true for housing. In ancient times, the method of building houses had a fixed procedure, and the equipment inside was also limited. Guan Zhong assisted Duke Huan, dominated the princes, rectified the world, and respected the royal family. History praised him greatly, but the house he lived in was criticized because it exceeded the limit. (Three returns and back stains) As for transportation, the ancients were also very particular about it, with fixed rules for seniority. You must walk on the main road, the so-called "Do not take shortcuts." You must walk on the right path, the so-called "Li Ming Sheng Mu, Zeng Zi did not enter." "The town called Chaoge, Mo Zhai returned the car," it can be seen that the ancients' activities in clothing, food, housing, and transportation were all in rules. Is the lifestyle rule talked about in the New Life Movement so strict? Because of this, although the Chinese society in the past did not have a community organization, and did not have precise laws, but because there were strict rules in the lifestyle, although the society had no formal organization, it had a spiritual union, so the society was not chaotic, and the order was quite solemn. This is all the rule of life, that is, maintaining society with etiquette, and its effectiveness is universal and deep, and it is greater than the law. The law sometimes ends, but the power of etiquette is to impress people invisibly. However, this kind of rule, with excessive red tape, can be done in the leisure class of feudal society. To implement it in today's society, many things are also felt to be out of line with modern life, so we want to promote a new life.

Spring and Autumn Notes of a Princess's Perfume Record by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou: The internal space of this locomotive seemed to be twice as large as that of an ordinary locomotive; otherwise, how could it accommodate seven workers inside? - Although, in fact, not all seven people were working. In the half of the service car behind the coal-water car, you couldn't find a stool, a chair, or a table, in order to prevent these workers from sitting down privately when no one was paying attention. Now, let's talk about the eunuch-style palace robes worn by these workers. Of course, they absolutely couldn't keep these clothes clean. In less than half a day, they were covered in soot and grease. When this happened, they had to change immediately. The old ones were thrown out of the car - no one would have thought that this was the clothing worn by a train worker - and new ones were put on. These expenses were all borne by the Ministry of Interior. Then, readers may ask, why didn't the workers take such good clothes back and wash them clean, even if they were stained with grease? However, they also knew that after this time, they didn't know when they would drive the train for the Empress Dowager again; and in ordinary times, they would be ridiculed by their relatives and friends if they wore such clothes. Originally, they were not worthy to wear them! Before the Empress Dowager started the train, she knew almost all the important points of how the train would move; although she had never personally visited the locomotive, she had asked all the questions she wanted to ask, and she had also ordered the train to run forward and backward in front of her, so she believed that this train would not cause her any danger. Another point is also very interesting. Her memory was particularly strong. Months later, she could often tell people in great detail about the various situations she had experienced on the train, and they were all very minute. (21)

China is Not Easy to Understand by Xun Zi: Pearl S. Buck, the pride of the American literary world, is an American woman who grew up in China. Her works, because they are all set in China and suit the curious appetite of Americans, are popular for a while. She not only drew huge royalties but also won some kind of award, which can be said to be a win-win for fame and fortune! However, although her works understand China better than ordinary European and American writers, the materials she uses are nothing more than the tyranny of warlords, the frequency of floods and droughts, and the suffering of peasants. In other words, she still depicts the ugly side of China! However, there are many people in the Chinese literary world who praise this foreign female writer. China is really difficult to understand, and it deserves the title of a mysterious ancient country in the East. Ms. Pearl S. Buck not only saw the ugly side of China, but she grew up in China and thought that she had a deep understanding of the lives of the Chinese people, but sometimes she still doesn't get the right answer. Recently, someone translated her article [Mother] in the Evening News. In describing the mother after giving birth, it said that she fell into a deep sleep; - I have read the original text, but I have forgotten it. The general meaning is like this, which is correct - This is completely wrong with the Chinese habit of giving birth. According to the old Chinese habit, after a woman gives birth, she must hold up her upper body and not be allowed to fall asleep within 24 hours. Traditional habits tell them that if they fall asleep, the blood stasis will rise and it will be fatal; unless Western-style childbirth is used recently, the doctor gives the parturient a shot before she is allowed to fall asleep. It is not easy to understand another country, especially for foreigners in general for China!

Smoking by Gu She: Smoking can be said to be the most artistic life, and it can also be said to be the most meaningful life. Think about it, with a cigarette in hand, leisurely reverie, watching the circles of smoke, forgetting the favor and humiliation of the world. Especially on a windy and rainy night, or when several people talk together, or when one person sits alone, it is simply necessary to smoke at this time. If you don’t smoke, I’m afraid you will feel insecure. Therefore, some people call cigarettes, alcohol, and tea the flavors of life, and I think cigarettes can especially be called the monosodium glutamate of monosodium glutamate. Because he can give people a particularly large number of stimulating opportunities, therefore, his monosodium glutamate effect is also particularly large. It can be rightly called the monosodium glutamate of monosodium glutamate in life. People who don’t smoke won’t know the wonderfulness of smoking. The wonderfulness of smoking cannot be described in words. If you don’t believe it, go and try it. As long as you are just addicted, this wonderfulness will gradually [麻着些儿 up] From then on, you will feel that you must smoke after a meal, and you must smoke when going to the toilet. This is still the beginning. Later, you will smoke when reading a book, smoke when reading a newspaper, smoke when writing an article, and especially smoke when sitting alone and thinking. As for good times and beautiful scenery, when you are happy, you must smoke even more. In short, you must smoke in any environment. At this time, you are old enough, and at the same time, you can fully appreciate the wonderfulness of smoking. The taste of cigarettes is bitter and spicy, which is most hated by people who don’t smoke. However, because the taste of cigarettes is bitter and spicy, the wonderfulness of smoking is so intense.

Local Supplement of the Shenbao Newspaper on [Standards]

Gu Yue

I have been fooled several times by [Standard Time], and today, due to a small matter, I needed to rush home by 2:30. The so-called [Standard Time] clock at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Donghongjiang Road clearly told me it was 1:20. However, the "[standard]" was thus ruined. When I got home, it was exactly 3:00. I am furious! Why call it [Standard]? Could it be that it differs from my home clock by a whole hour?

There are quite a few things called [Standard] now, such as [Standard Company], [Standard Beauty]... It's truly a dazzling array, everything you could want! However, after some investigation, the sports equipment from [Standard Company] doesn't seem any better than those bought from companies that aren't called [Standard], except the prices are higher! Everyone knows that [Standard Beauty] refers to Ms. Xu Lai of the Star Film Company, but I don't understand, is she [standard] in beauty? Character? Art? Too vague! [Standard] is too vague! Moreover, according to what my ears have heard, a star spends at least half of their monthly salary on publicity fees. How strange! Is [Standard Company] called [Standard] because its prices are high? Is [Standard Beauty] called [Standard] because she's willing to spend on publicity? Unreasonable [standards] should be overthrown! Too vague [standards] should be eliminated! At the same time, can [standards] that don't live up to their name still hide away and enjoy their reputation?

From this, we can predict the future of [Standards]. In the near future, we can imagine [Standard Theater], [Standard School], [Standard City], [Standard Province], [Standard National Salvation], shouting all sorts of slogans, the most [standard] [Standard XX]. Yes, perhaps [Standard] will be used in repetition because they think one [Standard] isn't enough to describe its [standard]! [Standard] loses its true meaning and becomes a sacrifice that doesn't live up to its name!

Let's analyze [Standard] further. [Biao] means [Target], [Zhun] means [Accurate], no doubt, everyone knows that! Of course, [Standard] means [Having an accurate target], neither leaning to the left nor leaning to the right, without the slightest error! You say the fulcrum of a balance scale is extremely [standard], absolutely not! Because human ideals are never so perfectly accurate! [Standard] is so rare! How can [Standard] be used carelessly!

Perhaps in the future, [Standard] will be used in reverse by humans, [Standard] becoming [Zhun Biao]! Because humans are inherently contradictory! The more novel, the more it can capture people's attention!

Advertising is becoming more and more sophisticated, and its applications are becoming more and more ingenious! [Standard] is certainly one of the things being exploited, and people's minds are being deceived, truly! Society is full of deception, I feel!

Using deceptive means for the promotion of goods, to attract attention, exploiting the sacredness of [Standard], can still be forgiven! Aimless deception! While exploiting [Standard], that is detestable! That should be a great sin! Because it's dereliction of duty, unwilling to take responsibility! Abandoning one's duty is the source of human sin!

I pity [Standard]'s pure character being sacrificed in this way! I am not just complaining about being late! I just feel it's too pitiful! God's darling! [Standard]!

The Magnet Stone

Ms. Ying

Peach blossoms blooming, willow branches swaying, aren't these two angels representing the arrival of spring in the world?

Yes; the chilling winter has quietly departed, and the bright spring has drifted in. At that time, everything, whether man or woman, is full of seductive allure, driving the other party into a dizzy and disoriented state, even neglecting sleep and food, becoming gaunt and thin. Indeed; this fact tells us very clearly - look!

Women, in the spring sunshine, strip off all the animal skins covering their limbs, replacing them with a close-fitting white gauze cheongsam full of mystery and allure. Whether she is sitting in a car, crossing a bare, pink leg, her mercury-like eyes constantly flirting in all directions, or walking down the street, her high-perched breasts rising and falling like waves, her full hips ceaselessly rotating, rotating. Add to that a smile, even if unintentional, and it will hook your soul to the ninth heaven. Once hooked, your soul will never return, forever and ever following her.

Men, in the spring sunshine, put on a brand new suit, a blood-red bow tie on a snow-white collar. The crimson sunlight enveloping them makes the red look even redder and the white even whiter. Shiny leather shoes, curled oily hair, dazzlingly eye-catching. Whether strolling in a public place or at a crossroads, he can win their hearts. As long as he makes a funny face, then the depths of their hearts will invisibly ripple, and their oval faces will also subtly blush. Naturally! At this time when love is budding and blooming, how could they not want to talk about love? How could they not want to XX? However, they only do it in their hearts? The fire of youth, its power is great! Great! The fire of youth!

Novel Tomorrow (3)

Mu Lin

The day before yesterday, I finished writing my diary and went to bed at two o'clock. Mom was already sound asleep, but I couldn't fall asleep no matter what. My hands and feet were cold, and my face was hot. I probably went to bed too late and had a fever. Luckily Mom didn't know, or she would nag again.

The more I couldn't sleep, the more I wanted to sleep, and the more I wanted to sleep, the less I could sleep. Staring blankly at the top of the mosquito net, I vaguely thought of him again. It was as if we were still in the movie theater, but my older sister had left at some point. He leaned close to me, and when the male and female leads on the screen were flirting, he explained the dialogue to me in detail, and made gestures like this and that. I knew he was doing it on purpose, but there was no room to move, so I pretended to be watching the movie and ignored him. However, he boldly grabbed my hand. I glanced at him, but he didn't seem to notice and squeezed even tighter. I wanted to pull it back, but being held by him like that felt strangely comfortable, my heart was pounding, as if I had been electrocuted, and I knew my cheeks must be as red as roses. I didn't dare to turn my head. From the corner of my eye, I saw his eyes gleaming and as terrifying as a tiger. Would he not make any other moves? Thinking like this, I exerted effort to pull my hand back. Sure enough, he pounced on me like a sheep and embraced my body. I was so scared that I cried for help.

Waking up, it was just a dream. My body was drenched in cold sweat, and after a while, it was as hot as fire. I looked at my hands and laughed, why would I have such a frightening dream for no reason? He is my older sister's husband, they love her so much, they are preparing to have children, I can't have delusional thoughts, I want to confess to my older sister, condemn myself, and then quietly fall asleep again.

When Mom woke me up, it was already ten o'clock in the morning. She stood in front of my mosquito net and smiled, scolding me for being a lazy girl and sleeping until this time without wanting to get up. I replied that I didn't feel well. She dropped her smile and reached out to my forehead to test it, [Ah Ying, you have a fever, you must have caught a cold last night. I don't know what time you went to bed? Just lie down quietly for a while.] She tucked the quilt around me and busied herself preparing some Wu Shi Tea, Mom always uses this method to treat fevers. I wanted to reply that it was okay, I would get up in a while, but Mom had already left the bedroom.

In the afternoon, I heard Mom talking to someone in the outer room. I thought he had come, so I deliberately coughed loudly, and then I heard Mom ask me, [Ah Ying, do you want tea?] But the second voice disappointed me, it wasn't him, but a voice that was also familiar said, [Really, Miss is sick.]

Mom brought the teacup in, and I asked her who was outside. Mom didn't answer, handed me the teacup, reached out to my forehead and tested it, saying, [Ah Ying, the fever has gone down, sleep well, don't think wildly.]

Having done something guilty myself, it seemed like every word had a thorn. I wanted to ask Mom what she meant by "thinking wildly", but she seemed to have something important to do and went to the outer room, talking to the person I couldn't remember for a moment, their voices even lower and I couldn't make out what they were saying.
