Japanese Athletes Set New World Swimming Records Again 204

(Osaka, Japanese United Press, 26th) As the Far Eastern Games are rapidly approaching, the Japanese swimming team held a record competition at the Koshien Indoor Swimming Pool (25 meters long) at 6 PM on the 25th. On this day, each athlete gave their all to test their abilities, resulting in six new world records and two new Japanese records. In the 800-meter event, which had previously yielded poor results, Makino, Kitamura, and Honda shortened the time to just over nine minutes. Koike broke his own world record in the 200-meter breaststroke, setting an amazing new record of 2 minutes 36.4 seconds. The main results of the day are as follows:

200-Meter Freestyle 205

2 minutes 10.4 seconds (New Japanese Record)

100-Meter Backstroke Kawazu 206

1 minute 8.4 seconds (New Japanese Record)

800-Meter Freestyle 207

(1) Makino 9 minutes 49.8 seconds

(2) Kitamura 9 minutes 51.8 seconds

(3) Honda 9 minutes 53.8 seconds

(These three results all broke the world record of 10 minutes 8.6 seconds)

200-Meter Breaststroke Koike 208

2 minutes 36.4 seconds

(Broke the world record of 2 minutes 42.6 seconds)

400-Meter Freestyle 209

(1) Yokoyama 4 minutes 45.8 seconds

(2) Ishiharada 4 minutes 46.2 seconds

(Both broke the world record of 4 minutes 46.4 seconds)

Zhijiang Track and Field Team Arrives in Shanghai This Afternoon; Volleyball Team Accompanies the Army 210

The track and field team from Zhijiang College of Arts and Sciences in Hangzhou is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon. The group consists of over 30 people and will stay at Shanghai University. They are scheduled to compete against the track and field team of Shanghai University in Yangshupu at the Shanghai University sports field on the 28th. Zhijiang is renowned in Hangzhou, and at the Zhejiang Provincial Games last year, its athletes set several new records. However, Shanghai University is also considered strong in Shanghai. The competition between the two sides is bound to be spectacular. Sports-loving readers should not miss the opportunity to drive out and watch.

At the same time, the Zhijiang volleyball team is also scheduled to go on the expedition with the army and has arranged friendly matches with Jiaotong University and Shanghai University. Shanghai University and Jiaotong University have a long history in Shanghai, while Zhijiang has always been the leader in Hangzhou. Furthermore, they have several outstanding athletes from Guangdong this semester, who are good at both offense and defense. It is uncertain who will emerge victorious when these strong rivals meet on that day.

Japanese Cabinet Meeting: Saito Advocates Participation, but the Military Expresses Opposition; Soldiers Want to Interfere with Sports – Track and Field Athletes Beaten in the Dark 211

(Tokyo, Japanese United Press, 26th) The early cabinet meeting today began at 2:20 PM. Prime Minister Saito, in his capacity as concurrently serving as the Minister of Education, discussed the issue of attending the Far Eastern Games, stating that since the government has already subsidized the expenses for sending athletes to the Far Eastern Games, it should be considered an established policy and hopes to send athletes as usual.

Military Opposes Participation 212

(Hualian News Agency, Tokyo Correspondent)

After the Shanghai Round Table Conference rejected the participation of the puppet Manchukuo in this Far Eastern Games, the Ministry of the Army was particularly indignant. On the 21st, officer corps within the Tokyo Garrison Headquarters and the First Division submitted rebuttals to Saito, who also serves as the Minister of Education, and the Japan Athletic Association. Also on the 21st, Ono, the gymnastics section chief of the Army Toyama School, convened an emergency meeting of the school's physical education and martial arts instructors. The result was the belief that the participation of Japanese athletes in this Far Eastern Games was a humiliating participation. The officer corps of the school also met at a certain location in the city that night and, after consultation, adopted a common approach with Ono's faction. On the 23rd, they visited Hiranuma, the president of the Athletic Association, and the Ministry of Education to express their opposition to participating in the games. On the other hand, they also sent people to contact nationalistic groups at various universities, guiding the athletic departments of the universities to resolve to oppose participation in the games. The military has extended its coercive hand, and the participation of Japanese athletes in the Far Eastern Games may be aborted. (Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 26th) Lieutenant Colonel Ono, the gymnastics section chief of the Army Toyama School, and other officers held another meeting last night and resolved to oppose the participation of Japanese athletes in the Far Eastern Games. They immediately sent a representative to meet with Principal Fukazawa, seeking his consent. This morning, a statement was issued in the name of the school, opposing the participation of Japanese athletes in the Far Eastern Games.

Athletic Association Encourages Athletes 213

(Dentsu, 26th, Tokyo) The preparatory committee of the Athletic Association for the Far Eastern Games sent an encouraging telegram yesterday to the delegation of athletes gathered in Kobe awaiting departure. The telegram stated that there seem to be various rumors before departure, and it is hoped that they will not be misled and will single-mindedly fulfill the duty of athletes. Regarding the Emperor's Cup, because the Shanghai Conference has decided to abolish the comprehensive athlete system, there is a strong opinion that it is not necessary to maintain the policy. They will first contact the Philippines, the host country, to discuss the method of handling it. Also, there are rumors that Tsuruoka Eikichi, the general manager of the swimming representatives, will resign, but he has denied this.

Athletes Beaten in the Dark 214

(Japanese United Press, 26th)

Osaka) Last night, while the Far Eastern Games track and field athletes Ono (hurdles), Suzuki (javelin), Akabane (javelin), Liu John (discus), and Ogura (decathlon) were taking a walk near the Koshien dormitory, more than a dozen thugs suddenly jumped out of the darkness, all wielding wooden sticks and hitting the athletes indiscriminately. Ono and Suzuki suffered injuries to their right feet, and Akabane's clothes were torn. People inside the dormitory, hearing the emergency, reported to the police department and requested that police officers be dispatched to guard them. Such an ominous incident has occurred in the sacred world of sports, and its impact on the Far Eastern Games is quite worrisome.
